           } else |_| {}\n            }\n\n            entries[i] = .{\n                .id = issue.id,\n                .title = issue.title,\n                .issue_type = issue.issue_type.toString(),\n                .closed_at = closed_at_str,\n                .close_reason = issue.close_reason,\n                .labels = issue.labels,\n            };\n        }\n\n        try ctx.output.printJson(ChangelogResult{\n            .success = true,\n            .entries = entries,\n            .count = filtered_issues.items.len,\n        });\n    } else {\n        if (filtered_issues.items.len == 0) {\n            if (!global.quiet) {\n                try ctx.output.info(\"No closed issues found\", .{});\n            }\n            return;\n        }\n\n        // Group by issue type if requested\n        if (changelog_args.group_by) |group| {\n            if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(group, \"type\")) {\n                try printGroupedByType(&ctx.output, filtered_issues.items, allocator);\n                return;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Default: print as a simple changelog list\n        try ctx.output.println(\"# Changelog\", .{});\n        try ctx.output.println(\"\", .{});\n\n        for (filtered_issues.items) |issue| {\n            const type_str = issue.issue_type.toString();\n            const reason_suffix = if (issue.close_reason) |r| blk: {\n                var buf: [256]u8 = undefined;\n                const result = std.fmt.bufPrint(&buf, \" ({s})\", .{r}) catch \"\";\n                break :blk result;\n            } else \"\";\n\n            try ctx.output.println(\"- [{s}] {s}: {s}{s}\", .{\n                issue.id,\n                type_str,\n                issue.title,\n                reason_suffix,\n            });\n        }\n\n        if (!global.quiet) {\n            try ctx.output.println(\"\", .{});\n            try ctx.output.info(\"{d} closed issue(s)\", .{filtered_issues.items.len});\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn printGroupedByType(output: *common.Output, issues: []Issue, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !void {\n    // Group issues by type\n    var type_groups: std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(std.ArrayListUnmanaged(Issue)) = .{};\n    defer {\n        var it = type_groups.valueIterator();\n        while (it.next()) |list| {\n            list.deinit(allocator);\n        }\n        type_groups.deinit(allocator);\n    }\n\n    for (issues) |issue| {\n        const type_str = issue.issue_type.toString();\n        const result = type_groups.getOrPut(allocator, type_str) catch continue;\n        if (!result.found_existing) {\n            result.value_ptr.* = .{};\n        }\n        result.value_ptr.append(allocator, issue) catch continue;\n    }\n\n    try output.println(\"# Changelog\", .{});\n    try output.println(\"\", .{});\n\n    // Print in a consistent order\n    const type_order = [_][]const u8{ \"feature\", \"bug\", \"task\", \"chore\", \"docs\", \"epic\", \"question\" };\n\n    for (type_order) |type_str| {\n        if (type_groups.get(type_str)) |group| {\n            if (group.items.len > 0) {\n                try output.println(\"## {s}\", .{type_str});\n                try output.println(\"\", .{});\n                for (group.items) |issue| {\n                    try output.println(\"- [{s}] {s}\", .{ issue.id, issue.title });\n                }\n                try output.println(\"\", .{});\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Print any remaining types not in the order list\n    var it = type_groups.iterator();\n    while (it.next()) |entry| {\n        var found = false;\n        for (type_order) |t| {\n            if (std.mem.eql(u8, entry.key_ptr.*, t)) {\n                found = true;\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n        if (!found and entry.value_ptr.items.len > 0) {\n            try output.println(\"## {s}\", .{entry.key_ptr.*});\n            try output.println(\"\", .{});\n            for (entry.value_ptr.items) |issue| {\n                try output.println(\"- [{s}] {s}\", .{ issue.id, issue.title });\n            }\n            try output.println(\"\", .{});\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nfn parseDateToTimestamp(date_str: []const u8) ?i64 {\n    // Parse YYYY-MM-DD format to Unix timestamp\n    if (date_str.len < 10) return null;\n\n    const year = std.fmt.parseInt(i32, date_str[0..4], 10) catch return null;\n    const month = std.fmt.parseInt(u4, date_str[5..7], 10) catch return null;\n    const day = std.fmt.parseInt(u5, date_str[8..10], 10) catch return null;\n\n    // Simple epoch calculation (not accounting for leap seconds)\n    const epoch_day = epochDayFromDate(year, month, day);\n    return epoch_day * 86400;\n}\n\nfn epochDayFromDate(year: i32, month: u4, day: u5) i64 {\n    // Days since Unix epoch (1970-01-01)\n    var y = @as(i64, year);\n    var m = @as(i64, month);\n    const d = @as(i64, day);\n\n    // Adjust for months\n    if (m <= 2) {\n        y -= 1;\n        m += 12;\n    }\n\n    const era: i64 = @divFloor(y, 400);\n    const yoe: i64 = @mod(y, 400);\n    const doy: i64 = @divFloor(153 * (m - 3) + 2, 5) + d - 1;\n    const doe: i64 = yoe * 365 + @divFloor(yoe, 4) - @divFloor(yoe, 100) + doy;\n\n    return era * 146097 + doe - 719468;\n}\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest findCommand(name: []const u8) ?*const CommandHelp {\n   690→    for (&commands) |*cmd| {\n   691→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd.name, name)) {\n   692→            return cmd;\n   693→        }\n   694→        for (cmd.aliases) |alias| {\n   695→            if (std.mem.eql(u8, alias, name)) {\n   696→                return cmd;\n   697→            }\n   698→        }\n   699→    }\n   700→    return null;\n   701→}\n   702→\n   703→/// Run the help command.\n   704→pub fn run(topic: ?[]const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !void {\n   705→    const stdout = std.fs.File.stdout();\n   706→    if (topic) |t| {\n   707→        try showCommandHelp(t, stdout, allocator);\n   708→    } else {\n   709→        try showGeneralHelp(stdout);\n   710→    }\n   711→}\n   712→\n   713→fn 800→        \\\\Run 'bz help <command>' for command-specific help.\n   801→        \\\\\n   802→    );\n   803→}\n   804→\n   805→fn showCommandHelp(name: []const u8, file: std.fs.File, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !void {\n   806→    const cmd = findCommand(name) orelse {\n   807→        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"Unknown command: {s}\\n\\n\", .{name});\n   808→        defer allocator.free(msg);\n   809→        try file.writeAll(msg);\n   810→        try file.writeAll(\"Run 'bz help' for a list of available commands.\\n\");\n   811→        return;\n   812→    };\n   813→\n   814→    // Command name and aliases\n   815→    try file.writeAll(cmd.name);\n   816→    if (cmd.aliases.len > 0) {\n   817→        try file.writeAll(\" (\");\n   818→        for (cmd.aliases, 0..) |alias, i| {\n   819→            if (i > 0) try file.writeAll(\", \");\n   820→            try file.writeAll(alias);\n   821→        }\n   822→        try file.writeAll(\")\");\n   823→    }\n   824→    try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   825→\n   826→    // Summary\n   827→    try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   828→    try file.writeAll(cmd.summary);\n   829→    try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   830→\n   831→    // Usage\n   832→    try file.writeAll(\"\\nUSAGE:\\n  \");\n   833→    try file.writeAll(cmd.usage);\n   834→    try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   835→\n   836→    // Description\n   837→    if (cmd.description.len > 0) {\n   838→        try file.writeAll(\"\\nDESCRIPTION:\\n\");\n   839→        try writeWrapped(file, cmd.description, 2, 78, allocator);\n   840→    }\n   841→\n   842→    // Arguments\n   843→    if (cmd.arguments.len > 0) {\n   844→        try file.writeAll(\"\\nARGUMENTS:\\n\");\n   845→        for (cmd.arguments) |arg| {\n   846→            const req = if (arg.required) \" (required)\" else \" (optional)\";\n   847→            const line = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"  {s}{s}\\n\", .{ arg.name, req });\n   848→            defer allocator.free(line);\n   849→            try file.writeAll(line);\n   850→            const desc = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"      {s}\\n\", .{arg.description});\n   851→            defer allocator.free(desc);\n   852→            try file.writeAll(desc);\n   853→        }\n   854→    }\n   855→\n   856→    // Flags\n   857→    if (cmd.flags.len > 0) {\n   858→        try file.writeAll(\"\\nFLAGS:\\n\");\n   859→        for (cmd.flags) |flag| {\n   860→            if (flag.short) |short| {\n   861→                const line = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"  {s}, {s}\", .{ short, flag.long });\n   862→                defer allocator.free(line);\n   863→                try file.writeAll(line);\n   864→            } else {\n   865→                const line = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"      {s}\", .{flag.long});\n   866→                defer allocator.free(line);\n   867→                try file.writeAll(line);\n   868→            }\n   869→            if (flag.arg) |arg| {\n   870→                const argline = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \" <{s}>\", .{arg});\n   871→                defer allocator.free(argline);\n   872→                try file.writeAll(argline);\n   873→            }\n   874→            try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   875→            const desc = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"      {s}\\n\", .{flag.description});\n   876→            defer allocator.free(desc);\n   877→            try file.writeAll(desc);\n   878→        }\n   879→    }\n   880→\n   881→    // Examples\n   882→    if (cmd.examples.len > 0) {\n   883→        try file.writeAll(\"\\nEXAMPLES:\\n\");\n   884→        for (cmd.examples) |ex| {\n   885→            const cmd_line = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"  $ {s}\\n\", .{ex.command});\n   886→            defer allocator.free(cmd_line);\n   887→            try file.writeAll(cmd_line);\n   888→            const desc_line = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"    {s}\\n\\n\", .{ex.description});\n   889→            defer allocator.free(desc_line);\n   890→            try file.writeAll(desc_line);\n   891→        }\n   892→    }\n   893→\n   894→    // See also\n   895→    if (cmd.see_also.len > 0) {\n   896→        try file.writeAll(\"SEE ALSO:\\n  \");\n   897→        for (cmd.see_also, 0..) |ref, i| {\n   898→            if (i > 0) try file.writeAll(\", \");\n   899→            try file.writeAll(ref);\n   900→        }\n   901→        try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   902→    }\n   903→}\n   904→\n   905→/// Write text with word wrapping.\n   906→fn writeWrapped(file: std.fs.File, text: []const u8, indent: usize, max_width: usize, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !void {\n   907→    const effective_width = max_width - indent;\n   908→\n   909→    // Pre-allocate indent string\n   910→    const indent_str = try allocator.alloc(u8, indent);\n   911→    defer allocator.free(indent_str);\n   912→    @memset(indent_str, ' ');\n   913→\n   914→    var line_start: usize = 0;\n   915→    var last_space: ?usize = null;\n   916→    var col: usize = 0;\n   917→\n   918→    for (text, 0..) |c, i| {\n   919→        if (c == ' ') {\n   920→            last_space = i;\n   921→        }\n   922→        col += 1;\n   923→\n   924→        if (col >= effective_width) {\n   925→            const break_at = last_space orelse i;\n   926→            try file.writeAll(indent_str);\n   927→            try file.writeAll(text[line_start..break_at]);\n   928→            try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   929→\n   930→            line_start = break_at + 1;\n   931→            col = i - break_at;\n   932→            last_space = null;\n   933→        }\n   934→    }\n   935→\n   936→    if (line_start < text.len) {\n   937→        try file.writeAll(indent_str);\n   938→        try file.writeAll(text[line_start..]);\n   939→        try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n   940→    }\n   941→}\n   942→\n   943→// Tests\n   944→\n   945→test \"findCommand finds by name\" {\n   946→    const cmd = findCommand(\"create\");\n   947→    try std.testing.expect(cmd != null);\n   948→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"create\", cmd.?.name);\n   949→}\n   950→\n   951→test \"findCommand finds by alias\" {\n   952→    const cmd = findCommand(\"add\");\n   953→    try std.testing.expect(cmd != null);\n   954→    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"create\", cmd.?.name);\n   955→}\n   956→\n   957→test \"findCommand returns null for unknown\" {\n   958→    const cmd = findCommand(\"nonexistent\");\n   959→    try std.testing.expect(cmd == null);\n   960→}\n   961→\n   962→test \"findCommand finds all main commands\" {\n   963→    // Verify a sampling of commands can be found\n   964→    try     },\n    },\n};\n\n/// Find help for a specific command (including aliases).\nfn findCommand(name: []const u8) ?*const CommandHelp {\n    for (&commands) |*cmd| {\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd.name, name)) {\n            return cmd;\n        }\n        for (cmd.aliases) |alias| {\n            if (std.mem.eql(u8, alias, name)) {\n                return cmd;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n    return null;\n}\n\n/// Run the help command.\npub fn run(topic: ?[]const u8, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !void {\n    const stdout = std.fs.File.stdout();\n    if (topic) |t| {\n        try showCommandHelp(t, stdout, allocator);\n    } else {\n        try showGeneralHelp(stdout);\n    }\n}\n\nfn showGeneralHelp(file: std.fs.File) !void {\n    try file.writeAll(\n        \\\\bz - checks\n        \\\\    config            Manage configuration\n        \\\\    sync              Sync with JSONL file\n        \\\\    orphans           Find issues with missing parent refs\n        \\\\    lint              Validate database consistency\n        \\\\\n        \\\\  Issue Management:\n        \\\\    create <title>    Create new issue\n        \\\\    q <title>         Quick capture (create + print ID only)\n        \\\\    show <id>         Show issue details\n        \\\\    update <id>       Update issue fields\n        \\\\    close <id>        Close an issue\n        \\\\    reopen <id>       Reopen a closed issue\n        \\\\    delete <id>       Soft delete (tombstone)\n        \\\\    defer <id>        Defer an issue\n        \\\\    undefer <id>      Remove deferral from an issue\n        \\\\\n        \\\\  Batch Operations:\n        \\\\    add-batch         Create issues from stdin/file (single lock)\n        \\\\    import <file>     Import issues \\\\  --no-auto-flush   Skip automatic JSONL export\n        \\\\  --no-auto-import  Skip JSONL freshness check\n        \\\\\n        \\\\Run 'bz help <command>' for command-specific help.\n        \\\\\n    );\n}\n\nfn showCommandHelp(name: []const u8, file: std.fs.File, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !void {\n    const cmd = findCommand(name) orelse {\n        const msg = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"Unknown command: {s}\\n\\n\", .{name});\n        defer allocator.free(msg);\n        try file.writeAll(msg);\n        try file.writeAll(\"Run 'bz help' for a list of available commands.\\n\");\n        return;\n    };\n\n    // Command name and aliases\n    try file.writeAll(cmd.name);\n    if (cmd.aliases.len > 0) {\n        try file.writeAll(\" (\");\n        for (cmd.aliases, 0..) |alias, i| {\n            if (i > 0) try file.writeAll(\", \");\n            try file.writeAll(alias);\n        }\n        try file.writeAll(\")\");\n    }\n    try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n\n    // Summary\n    try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n    try file.writeAll(cmd.summary);\n    try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n\n    // Usage\n    try file.writeAll(\"\\nUSAGE:\\n  \");\n    try file.writeAll(cmd.usage);\n    try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n\n    // Description\n    if (cmd.description.len > 0) {\n        try file.writeAll(\"\\nDESCRIPTION:\\n\");\n        try writeWrapped(file, cmd.description, 2, 78, allocator);\n    }\n\n    // Arguments\n    if (cmd.arguments.len > 0) {\n        try file.writeAll(\"\\nARGUMENTS:\\n\");\n        for (cmd.arguments) |arg| {\n            const req = if (arg.required) \" (required)\" else \" (optional)\";\n            const line = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"  {s}{s}\\n\", .{ arg.name, req });\n            defer allocator.free(line);\n            try file.writeAll(line);\n            const desc = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"      {s}\\n\", .{arg.description});\n            defer allocator.free(desc);\n            try file.writeAll(desc);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Flags\n    if (cmd.flags.len > 0) {\n        try file.writeAll(\"\\nFLAGS:\\n\");\n        for (cmd.flags) |flag| {\n            if (flag.short) |short| {\n                const line = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"  {s}, {s}\", .{ short, flag.long });\n                defer allocator.free(line);\n                try file.writeAll(line);\n            } else {\n                const line = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"      {s}\", .{flag.long});\n                defer allocator.free(line);\n                try file.writeAll(line);\n            }\n            if (flag.arg) |arg| {\n                const argline = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \" <{s}>\", .{arg});\n                defer allocator.free(argline);\n                try file.writeAll(argline);\n            }\n            try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n            const desc = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"      {s}\\n\", .{flag.description});\n            defer allocator.free(desc);\n            try file.writeAll(desc);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Examples\n    if (cmd.examples.len > 0) {\n        try file.writeAll(\"\\nEXAMPLES:\\n\");\n        for (cmd.examples) |ex| {\n            const cmd_line = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"  $ {s}\\n\", .{ex.command});\n            defer allocator.free(cmd_line);\n            try file.writeAll(cmd_line);\n            const desc_line = try std.fmt.allocPrint(allocator, \"    {s}\\n\\n\", .{ex.description});\n            defer allocator.free(desc_line);\n            try file.writeAll(desc_line);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // See also\n    if (cmd.see_also.len > 0) {\n        try file.writeAll(\"SEE ALSO:\\n  \");\n        for (cmd.see_also, 0..) |ref, i| {\n            if (i > 0) try file.writeAll(\", \");\n            try file.writeAll(ref);\n        }\n        try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n    }\n}\n\n/// Write text with word wrapping.\nfn writeWrapped(file: std.fs.File, text: []const u8, indent: usize, max_width: usize, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !void {\n    const effective_width = max_width - indent;\n\n    // Pre-allocate indent string\n    const indent_str = try allocator.alloc(u8, indent);\n    defer allocator.free(indent_str);\n    @memset(indent_str, ' ');\n\n    var line_start: usize = 0;\n    var last_space: ?usize = null;\n    var col: usize = 0;\n\n    for (text, 0..) |c, i| {\n        if (c == ' ') {\n            last_space = i;\n        }\n        col += 1;\n\n        if (col >= effective_width) {\n            const break_at = last_space orelse i;\n            try file.writeAll(indent_str);\n            try file.writeAll(text[line_start..break_at]);\n            try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n\n            line_start = break_at + 1;\n            col = i - break_at;\n            last_space = null;\n        }\n    }\n\n    if (line_start < text.len) {\n        try file.writeAll(indent_str);\n        try file.writeAll(text[line_start..]);\n        try file.writeAll(\"\\n\");\n    }\n}\n\n// Tests\n\ntest \"findCommand finds by name\" {\n    const cmd = findCommand(\"create\");\n    try std.testing.expect(cmd != null);\n    try std.testing.expectEqualStrings(\"create\", cmd.?.name);\n}\n\ntest \"findCommand finds by alias\" {\n    const cmd = std.testing.expect(findCommand(\"update\") != null);\n    try std.testing.expect(findCommand(\"close\") != null);\n    try std.testing.expect(findCommand(\"dep\") != null);\n    try  format: BatchFormat = .titles, // Input format\n   159→};\n   160→\n   161→/// Batch input format.\n   162→pub const BatchFormat = enum {\n   163→    titles, // One title per line\n   164→    jsonl, // Full JSONL format (one issue per line)\n   165→\n   166→    pub fn fromString(s: []const u8) ?BatchFormat {\n   167→        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"titles\")) return .titles;\n   168→        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"jsonl\")) return .jsonl;\n   169→        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"json\")) return .jsonl;\n   170→        return null;\n   171→    }\n   172→};\n   173→\n   174→/// Import command arguments.\n   175→/// Imports issues from a JSONL file with single lock acquisition.\n   176→pub const ImportArgs = struct {\n   177→    file: []const u8, // Path to JSONL file (required)\n   178→    merge: bool = false, // Merge instead of replace\n   179→    dry_run: bool = false, // Show what would be imported without importing\n   180→};\n   181→\n   182→/// Sort field options for list command.\n   183→pub const SortField = enum {\n   184→    created_at,\n   185→    updated_at,\n   186→    priority,\n   187→\n   188→    pub fn fromString(s: []const u8) ?SortField {\n   189→        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"created\") or std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"created_at\")) return .created_at;\n   190→        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"updated\") or std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"updated_at\")) return .updated_at;\n   191→        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"priority\")) return .priority;\n   192→        return null;\n   193→    }\n   194→};\n   195→\n   196→/// List command arguments.\n   197→pub const ListArgs = struct {\n   198→    status: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   199→    priority: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   200→    issue_type: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   201→    assignee: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   202→    label: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   203→    limit: ?u32 = null,\n   204→    all: bool = false,\n   205→    sort: SortField = .created_at,\n   206→    sort_desc: bool = true,\n   207→};\n   208→\n   209→/// Ready command arguments.\n   210→pub const ReadyArgs = struct {\n   211→    limit: ?u32 = null,\n   212→};\n   213→\n   214→/// Blocked command arguments.\n   215→pub const BlockedArgs = struct {\n   216→    limit: ?u32 = null,\n   217→};\n   218→\n   219→/// Search command arguments.\n   220→pub const SearchArgs = struct {\n   221→    query: []const u8,\n   222→    limit: ?u32 = null,\n   223→};\n   224→\n   225→/// Stale command arguments.\n   226→pub const StaleArgs = struct {\n   227→    days: u32 = 30,\n   228→    limit: ?u32 = null,\n   229→};\n   230→\n   231→/// Count command arguments.\n   232→pub const CountArgs = struct {\n   233→    group_by: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   234→};\n   235→\n   236→/// Defer command arguments.\n   237→pub const DeferArgs = struct {\n   238→    id: []const u8,\n   239→    until: ?[]const u8 = null, // RFC3339 date or relative like \"+7d\"\n   240→    reason: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   241→};\n   242→\n   243→/// Undefer command arguments.\n   244→pub const UndeferArgs = struct {\n   245→    id: []const u8,\n   246→};\n   247→\n   248→/// Epic subcommand variants.\n   249→pub const EpicSubcommand = union(enum) {\n   250→    create: struct {\n   251→        title: []const u8,\n   252→        description: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   253→        priority: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   254→    },\n   255→    add: struct {\n   256→        epic_id: []const u8,\n   257→        issue_id: []const u8,\n   258→    },\n   259→    remove: struct {\n   260→        epic_id: []const u8,\n   261→        issue_id: []const u8,\n   262→    },\n   263→    list: struct {\n   264→        epic_id: []const u8,\n   265→    },\n   266→};\n   267→\n   268→/// Epic command arguments.\n   269→pub const EpicArgs = struct {\n   270→    subcommand: EpicSubcommand,\n   271→};\n   272→\n   273→/// Dependency subcommand variants.\n   274→pub const DepSubcommand = union(enum) {\n   275→    add: struct {\n   276→        child: []const u8,\n   277→        parent: []const u8,\n   278→        dep_type: []const u8 = \"blocks\",\n   279→    },\n   280→    remove: struct {\n   281→        child: []const u8,\n   282→        parent: []const u8,\n   283→    },\n   284→    list: struct {\n   285→        id: []const u8,\n   286→    },\n   287→    tree: struct {\n   288→        id: []const u8,\n   289→    },\n   290→    cycles: void,\n   291→};\n   292→\n   293→/// Dependency command arguments.\n   294→pub const DepArgs = struct {\n   295→    subcommand: DepSubcommand,\n   296→};\n   297→\n   298→/// Graph command (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"ascii\")) return .ascii;\n   305→        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"dot\")) return .dot;\n   306→        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"graphviz\")) return .dot;\n   307→        return null;\n   308→    }\n   309→};\n   310→\n   311→/// Graph command arguments.\n   312→pub const GraphArgs = struct {\n   313→    id: ?[]const u8 = null, // Optional: show graph for specific issue, otherwise show all\n   314→    format: GraphFormat = .ascii,\n   315→    depth: ?u32 = null, // Max depth for tree traversal\n   316→};\n   317→\n   318→/// Label subcommand variants.\n   319→pub const LabelSubcommand = union(enum) {\n   320→    add: struct {\n   321→        id: []const u8,\n   322→        labels: []const []const u8,\n   323→    },\n   324→    remove: 353→};\n   354→\n   355→/// History command arguments.\n   356→pub const HistoryArgs = struct {\n   357→    id: []const u8,\n   358→};\n   359→\n   360→/// Audit command arguments.\n   361→pub const \"type\")\n   371→};\n   372→\n   373→/// Sync command arguments.\n   374→pub const SyncArgs = struct {\n   375→    flush_only: bool = false,\n   376→    import_only: bool = false,\n   377→};\n   378→\n   379→/// Shell completion types.\n   380→pub const Shell = enum {\n   381→    bash,\n   382→    zsh,\n   383→    fish,\n   384→    powershell,\n   385→\n   386→    pub fn fromString(s: []const u8) ?Shell {\n   387→        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"bash\")) return .bash;\n   388→        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"zsh\")) return .zsh;\n   389→        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"fish\")) return .fish;\n   390→        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"powershell\")) return .powershell;\n   391→        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"ps\")) return .powershell;\n   392→        return null;\n   393→    }\n   394→};\n   395→\n   396→/// Completions command arguments.\n   397→pub const CompletionsArgs = struct {\n   398→    shell: Shell,\n   399→};\n   400→\n   401→/// Help command arguments.\n   402→pub const HelpArgs = struct {\n   403→    topic: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   404→};\n   405→\n   406→/// Config subcommand variants.\n   407→pub const ConfigSubcommand = union(enum) {\n   408→    get: struct {\n   409→        key: []const u8,\n   410→    },\n   411→    set: struct {\n   412→        key: []const u8,\n   413→        value: []const u8,\n   414→    },\n   415→    list: void,\n   416→};\n   417→\n   418→/// Config command arguments.\n   419→pub const ConfigArgs = struct {\n   420→    subcommand: ConfigSubcommand,\n   421→};\n   422→\n   423→/// Orphans command arguments.\n   424→pub const OrphansArgs = struct {\n   425→    limit: ?u32 = null,\n   426→    hierarchy_only: bool = false,\n   427→    deps_only: bool = false,\n   428→};\n   429→\n   430→/// Lint command arguments.\n   431→pub const LintArgs = struct {\n   432→    limit: ?u32 = null,\n   433→};\n   434→\n   435→/// Result of parsing command-line arguments.\n   436→pub const ParseResult = struct {\n   437→    global: GlobalOptions,\n   438→    command: Command,\n   439→\n   440→    /// Free any memory allocated during parsing (labels, deps slices).\n   441→    pub fn deinit(self: *ParseResult, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n   442→        switch (self.command) {\n   443→            .create => |create| {\n   444→                if (create.labels.len > 0) allocator.free(create.labels);\n   445→                if (create.deps.len > 0) allocator.free(create.deps);\n   446→            },\n   447→            .label => |label_cmd| {\n   448→                switch (label_cmd.subcommand) {\n   449→                    .add => |add| if (add.labels.len > 0) allocator.free(add.labels),\n   450→                    .remove => |remove| if (remove.labels.len > 0) allocator.free(remove.labels),\n   451→                    else => {},\n   452→                }\n   453→            },\n   454→            else => {},\n   455→        }\n   456→    }\n   457→};\n   458→\n   459→/// Errors that can occur during argument parsing.\n   460→pub const ParseError = error{\n   461→    UnknownCommand,\n   462→    MissingRequiredArgument,\n   463→    InvalidArgument,\n   464→    UnknownFlag,\n   465→    MissingFlagValue,\n   466→    InvalidFlagValue,\n   467→    InvalidShell,\n   468→    UnknownSubcommand,\n   469→};\n   470→\n   471→/// Command-line argument parser.\n   472→pub const ArgParser = struct {\n   473→    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n   474→    args: []const []const u8,\n   475→    index: usize = 0,\n   476→\n   477→    const Self = @This();\n   478→\n   479→    pub fn init(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, args: []const []const u8) Self {\n   480→        return .{\n   481→            .allocator = allocator,\n   482→            .args = args,\n   483→        };\n   484→    }\n   485→\n   486→    /// Parse all arguments into a ParseResult.\n   487→    pub fn parse(self: *Self) ParseError!ParseResult {\n   488→        var global = GlobalOptions{};\n   489→\n   490→        // Parse global flags first\n   491→        while (self.hasNext()) {\n   492→            const arg = self.peek().?;\n   493→            if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, arg, \"-\")) {\n   494→                if (self.parseGlobalFlag(&global)) |consumed| {\n   495→                    if (!consumed) break;\n   496→                } else |_| {\n   497→                    break;\n   498→                }\n   499→            } else {\n   500→                break;\n   501→            }\n   502→        }\n   503→\n   504→        // Parse subcommand\n   505→        const cmd_str = self.next() orelse {\n   506→            return .{\n   507→                .global = global,\n   508→                .command = .{ .help = .{ .topic = null } },\n   509→            };\n   510→        };\n   511→\n   512→        const command = try self.parseCommand(cmd_str);\n   513→\n   514→        return .{\n   515→            .global = global,\n   516→            .command = command,\n   517→        };\n   518→    }\n   519→\n   520→    fn parseGlobalFlag(self: *Self, global: *GlobalOptions) ParseError!bool {\n   521→        const arg = self.next().?;\n   522→\n   523→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--json\")) {\n   524→            global.json = true;\n   525→            return true;\n   526→        }\n   527→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--toon\")) {\n   528→            global.toon = true;\n   529→            return true;\n   530→        }\n   531→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-q\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--quiet\")) {\n   532→            global.quiet = true;\n   533→            return true;\n   534→        }\n   535→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-v\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--verbose\")) {\n   536→            global.verbose +|= 1;\n   537→            return true;\n   538→        }\n   539→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-vv\")) {\n   540→            global.verbose +|= 2;\n   541→            return true;\n   542→        }\n   543→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-color\")) {\n   544→            global.no_color = true;\n   545→            return true;\n   546→        }\n   547→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-auto-flush\")) {\n   548→            global.no_auto_flush = true;\n   549→            return true;\n   550→        }\n   551→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-auto-import\")) {\n   552→            global.no_auto_import = true;\n   553→            return true;\n   554→        }\n   555→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--data\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--db\")) {\n   556→            global.data_path = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   557→            return true;\n   558→        }\n   559→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--actor\")) {\n   560→            global.actor = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   561→            return true;\n   562→        }\n   563→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--lock-timeout\")) {\n   564→            const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   565→            global.lock_timeout = std.fmt.parseInt(u32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n   566→            return true;\n   567→        }\n   568→\n   569→        // Put back if not recognized\n   570→        self.index -= 1;\n   571→        return error.UnknownFlag;\n   572→    }\n   573→\n   574→    fn parseCommand(self: *Self, cmd: []const u8) ParseError!Command {\n   575→        // Workspace\n   576→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"init\")) {\n   577→            return .{ .init = try self.parseInitArgs() };\n   578→        }\n   579→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"info\")) {\n   580→            return .{ .info = {} };\n   581→        }\n   582→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"stats\")) {\n   583→            return .{ .stats = {} };\n   584→        }\n   585→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"doctor\")) {\n   586→            return .{ .doctor = {} };\n   587→        }\n   588→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"config\")) {\n   589→            return .{ .config = try self.parseConfigArgs() };\n   590→        }\n   591→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"orphans\")) {\n   592→            return .{ .orphans = try self.parseOrphansArgs() };\n   593→        }\n   594→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"lint\")) {\n   595→            return .{ .lint = try self.parseLintArgs() };\n   596→        }\n   597→\n   598→        // Issue CRUD\n   599→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"create\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"add\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"new\")) {\n   600→            return .{ .create = try self.parseCreateArgs() };\n   601→        }\n   602→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"q\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"quick\")) {\n   603→            return .{ .q = try self.parseQuickArgs() };\n   604→        }\n   605→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"show\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"get\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"view\")) {\n   606→            return .{ .show = try self.parseShowArgs() };\n   607→        }\n   608→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"update\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"edit\")) {\n   609→            return .{ .update = try self.parseUpdateArgs() };\n   610→        }\n   611→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"close\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"done\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"finish\")) {\n   612→            return .{ .close = try self.parseCloseArgs() };\n   613→        }\n   614→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"reopen\")) {\n   615→            return .{ .reopen = try self.parseReopenArgs() };\n   616→        }\n   617→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"delete\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"rm\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"remove\")) {\n   618→            return .{ .delete = try self.parseDeleteArgs() };\n   619→        }\n   620→\n   621→        // Batch Operations\n   622→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"add-batch\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"batch-add\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"batch\")) {\n   623→            return .{ .add_batch = try self.parseAddBatchArgs() };\n   624→        }\n   625→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"import\")) {\n   626→            return .{ .import_cmd = try self.parseImportArgs() };\n   627→        }\n   628→\n   629→        // Query\n   630→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"list\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"ls\")) {\n   631→            return .{ .list = try self.parseListArgs() };\n   632→        }\n   633→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"ready\")) {\n   634→            return .{ .ready = try self.parseReadyArgs() };\n   635→        }\n   636→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"blocked\")) {\n   637→            return .{ .blocked = try self.parseBlockedArgs() };\n   638→        }\n   639→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"search\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"find\")) {\n   640→            return .{ .search = try self.parseSearchArgs() };\n   641→        }\n   642→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"stale\")) {\n   643→            return .{ .stale = try self.parseStaleArgs() };\n   644→        }\n   645→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"count\")) {\n   646→            return .{ .count = try self.parseCountArgs() };\n   647→        }\n   648→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"defer\")) {\n   649→            return .{ .defer_cmd = try self.parseDeferArgs() };\n   650→        }\n   651→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"undefer\")) {\n   652→            return .{ .undefer = try self.parseUndeferArgs() };\n   653→        }\n   654→\n   655→        // Dependencies\n   656→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"dep\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"deps\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"dependency\")) {\n   657→            return .{ .dep = try self.parseDepArgs() };\n   658→        }\n   659→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"graph\")) {\n   660→            return .{ .graph = try self.parseGraphArgs() };\n   661→        }\n   662→\n   663→        // Epics\n   664→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"epic\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"epics\")) {\n   665→            return .{ .epic = try self.parseEpicArgs() };\n   666→        }\n   667→\n   668→        // Labels\n   669→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"label\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"labels\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"tag\")) {\n   670→            return .{ .label = try self.parseLabelArgs() };\n   671→        }\n   672→\n   673→        // Comments\n   674→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"comments\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"comment\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"note\")) {\n   675→            return .{ .comments = try self.parseCommentsArgs() };\n   676→        }\n   677→\n   678→        // Audit\n   679→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"history\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"log\")) {\n   680→            return .{ .history = try self.parseHistoryArgs() };\n   681→        }\n   682→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"audit\")) {\n   683→            return .{ .audit = try self.parseAuditArgs() };\n   684→        }\n   685→\n   686→        // Changelog\n   687→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"changelog\")) {\n   688→            return .{ .changelog = try self.parseChangelogArgs() };\n   689→        }\n   690→\n   691→        // Sync\n   692→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"sync\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"flush\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"export\")) {\n   693→            return .{ .sync = try self.parseSyncArgs() };\n   694→        }\n   695→\n   696→        // System\n   697→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"version\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"--version\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"-V\")) {\n   698→            return .{ .version = {} };\n   699→        }\n   700→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"schema\")) {\n   701→            return .{ .schema = {} };\n   702→        }\n   703→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"completions\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"completion\")) {\n   704→            return .{ .completions = try self.parseCompletionsArgs() };\n   705→        }\n   706→\n   707→        // Help\n   708→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"help\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"--help\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"-h\")) {\n   709→            return .{ .help = try self.parseHelpArgs() };\n   710→        }\n   711→\n   712→        return error.UnknownCommand;\n   713→    }\n   714→\n   715→    fn parseInitArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!InitArgs {\n   716→        var result = InitArgs{};\n   717→        while (self.hasNext()) {\n   718→            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--prefix\")) {\n   719→                result.prefix = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   720→            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n   721→                result.prefix = self.next().?;\n   722→            } else break;\n   723→        }\n   724→        return result;\n   725→    }\n   726→\n   727→    fn parseCreateArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!CreateArgs {\n   728→        var result = CreateArgs{ .title = undefined };\n   729→        var title_set = false;\n   730→        var labels: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n   731→        var deps: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n   732→\n   733→        while (self.hasNext()) {\n   734→            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-d\", \"--description\")) {\n   735→                result.description = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   736→            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-t\", \"--type\")) {\n   737→                result.issue_type = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   738→            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--priority\")) {\n   739→                result.priority = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   740→            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-a\", \"--assignee\")) {\n   741→                result.assignee = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n   742→            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-l\", \"--label\")) {\n   743→                labels.append(self.allocator, self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue) catch return |limit| {\n  1232→                result.limit = limit;\n  1233→            } else if (self.consumeFlag(null, \"--hierarchy-only\")) {\n  1234→                result.hierarchy_only = true;\n  1235→            } else if (self.consumeFlag(null, \"--deps-only\")) {\n  1236→                result.deps_only = true;\n  1237→            } else break;\n  1238→        }\n  1239→        return result;\n  1240→    }\n  1241→\n  1242→    fn parseLintArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!LintArgs {\n  1243→        var result = LintArgs{};\n  1244→        while (self.hasNext()) {\n  1245→            if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n  1246→                result.limit = limit;\n  1247→            } else break;\n  1248→        }\n  1249→        return result;\n  1250→    }\n  1251→\n  1252→    fn hasNext(self: *Self) bool {\n  1253→        return self.index < self.args.len;\n  1254→    }\n  1255→\n  1256→    fn peek(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n  1257→        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n  1258→        return self.args[self.index];\n  1259→    }\n  1260→\n  1261→    fn next(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n  1262→        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n  1263→        const arg = self.args[self.index];\n  1264→        self.index += 1;\n  1265→        return arg;\n  1266→    }\n  1267→\n  1268→    /// Skip a peeked argument (used after checking with peek() and wanting to consume it).\n  1269→    fn skip(self: *Self) void {\n  1270→        if (self.index < self.args.len) {\n  1271→            self.index += 1;\n  1272→        }\n  1273→    }\n  1274→\n  1275→    /// Check if current arg matches a flag, and if so consume it and return true.\n  1276→    fn consumeFlag(self: *Self, short: ?[]const u8, long: []const u8) bool {\n  1277→        const arg = self.peek() orelse return false;\n  1278→        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, long) or (short != null and std.mem.eql(u8, arg, short.?))) {\n  1279→            self.skip();\n  1280→            return true;\n  1281→        }\n  1282→        return false;\n  1283→    }\n  1284→\n  1285→    /// Parse a u32 value after consuming a flag. Returns null if missing, error if invalid.\n  1286→    fn consumeU32(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n  1287→        const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n  1288→        return std.fmt.parseInt(u32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n  1289→    }\n  1290→\n  1291→    /// Parse an optional --limit/-n flag, returning the value if present.\n  1292→    fn parseLimitFlag(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n  1293→        if (self.consumeFlag(\"-n\", \"--limit\")) {\n  1294→            return try self.consumeU32();\n  1295→        }\n  1296→        return null;\n  1297→    }\n  1298→\n  1299→    /// Returns the next arg if it's a positional (doesn't start with \"-\"), otherwise null.\n  1300→    fn peekPositional(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n  1301→        const arg = self.peek() orelse return null;\n  1302→        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, arg, \"-\")) return null;\n  1303→        return arg;\n  1304→    }\n  1305→};\n  1306→\n  1307→// Tests\n  1308→\n  1309→test \"parse no arguments shows help\" {\n  1310→    const args = [_][]const u8{};\n  1311→    var parser = ArgParser.init(std.testing.allocator, &args);\n  1312→    const result = try CLI argument parsing for beads_zig.\n//!\n//! Parses command-line arguments into structured data for command dispatch.\n//! Supports global flags, subcommands, and subcommand-specific arguments.\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\n\n/// Global CLI options that apply to all commands.\npub const GlobalOptions = struct {\n    json: bool = false,\n    toon: bool = false,\n    quiet: bool = false,\n    silent: bool = false, // Suppress ALL output including errors (for tests)\n    verbose: u8 = 0,\n    no_color: bool = false,\n    data_path: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    actor: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    lock_timeout: u32 = 5000,\n    no_auto_flush: bool = false,\n    no_auto_import: bool = false,\n\n    /// Returns true if structured output (JSON or TOON) is enabled.\n    pub fn isStructuredOutput(self: GlobalOptions) bool {\n        return self.json or self.toon;\n    }\n};\n\n/// All available subcommands.\npub const Command = union(enum) {\n    // Workspace\n    init: InitArgs,\n    info: void,\n    stats: void,\n    doctor: void,\n    config: ConfigArgs,\n    orphans: OrphansArgs,\n    lint: LintArgs,\n\n    // Issue CRUD\n    create: CreateArgs,\n    q: QuickArgs,\n    show: ShowArgs,\n    update: UpdateArgs,\n    close: CloseArgs,\n    reopen: ReopenArgs,\n    delete: DeleteArgs,\n\n    // Batch Operations\n    add_batch: AddBatchArgs,\n    import_cmd: ImportArgs,\n\n    // Query\n    list: ListArgs,\n    ready: ReadyArgs,\n    blocked: BlockedArgs,\n    search: SearchArgs,\n    stale: StaleArgs,\n    count: CountArgs,\n    defer_cmd: DeferArgs,\n    undefer: UndeferArgs,\n\n    // Dependencies\n    dep: DepArgs,\n    graph: GraphArgs,\n\n    // Epics\n    epic: EpicArgs,\n\n    // Labels\n    label: LabelArgs,\n\n    // Comments\n    comments: CommentsArgs,\n\n    // Audit\n    history: HistoryArgs,\n    audit: AuditArgs,\n\n    // Changelog\n    changelog: ChangelogArgs,\n\n    // Sync\n    sync: SyncArgs,\n\n    // System\n    version: void,\n    schema: void,\n    completions: CompletionsArgs,\n\n    // Help\n    help: HelpArgs,\n};\n\n/// Init command arguments.\npub const InitArgs = struct {\n    prefix: []const u8 = \"bd\",\n};\n\n/// Create command arguments.\npub const CreateArgs = struct {\n    title: []const u8,\n    description: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    issue_type: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    priority: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    assignee: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    labels: []const []const u8 = &[_][]const u8{},\n    deps: []const []const u8 = &[_][]const u8{},\n    due: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    estimate: ?i32 = null,\n};\n\n/// Quick capture command arguments.\npub const QuickArgs = struct {\n    title: []const u8,\n    priority: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\n/// Show command arguments.\npub const ShowArgs = struct {\n    id: []const u8,\n    with_comments: bool = true,\n    with_history: bool = false,\n};\n\n/// Update command arguments.\npub const UpdateArgs = struct {\n    id: []const u8,\n    title: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    description: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    issue_type: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    priority: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    assignee: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    status: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    /// Expected version for optimistic locking (compare-and-swap).\n    expected_version: ?u64 = null,\n};\n\n/// Close command arguments.\npub const CloseArgs = struct {\n    id: []const u8,\n    reason: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\n/// Reopen command arguments.\npub const ReopenArgs = struct {\n    id: []const u8,\n};\n\n/// Delete command arguments.\npub const DeleteArgs = struct {\n    id: []const u8,\n};\n\n/// Add-batch command arguments.\n/// Creates multiple issues from stdin or a file with single lock acquisition.\npub const AddBatchArgs = struct {\n    file: ?[]const u8 = null, // Read from file instead of stdin\n    format: BatchFormat = .titles, // Input format\n};\n\n/// Batch input format.\npub const BatchFormat = enum {\n    titles, // One title per line\n    jsonl, // Full JSONL format (one issue per line)\n\n    pub fn fromString(s: []const u8) ?BatchFormat {\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"titles\")) return .titles;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"jsonl\")) return .jsonl;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"json\")) return .jsonl;\n        return null;\n    }\n};\n\n/// Import command arguments.\n/// Imports issues from a JSONL file with single lock acquisition.\npub const ImportArgs = struct {\n    file: []const u8, // Path to JSONL file (required)\n    merge: bool = false, // Merge instead of replace\n    dry_run: bool = false, // Show what would be imported without importing\n};\n\n/// Sort field options for list command.\npub const SortField = enum {\n    created_at,\n    updated_at,\n    priority,\n\n    pub fn fromString(s: []const u8) ?SortField {\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"created\") or std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"created_at\")) return .created_at;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"updated\") or std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"updated_at\")) return .updated_at;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"priority\")) return .priority;\n        return null;\n    }\n};\n\n/// List command arguments.\npub const ListArgs = struct {\n    status: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    priority: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    issue_type: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    assignee: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    label: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n    all: bool = false,\n    sort: SortField = .created_at,\n    sort_desc: bool = true,\n};\n\n/// Ready command arguments.\npub const ReadyArgs = struct {\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n};\n\n/// Blocked command arguments.\npub const BlockedArgs = struct {\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n};\n\n/// Search command arguments.\npub const SearchArgs = struct {\n    query: []const u8,\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n};\n\n/// Stale command arguments.\npub const StaleArgs = struct {\n    days: u32 = 30,\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n};\n\n/// Count command arguments.\npub const CountArgs = struct {\n    group_by: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\n/// Defer command arguments.\npub const DeferArgs = struct {\n    id: []const u8,\n    until: ?[]const u8 = null, // RFC3339 date or relative like \"+7d\"\n    reason: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\n/// Undefer command arguments.\npub const UndeferArgs = struct {\n    id: []const u8,\n};\n\n/// Epic subcommand variants.\npub const EpicSubcommand = union(enum) {\n    create: struct {\n        title: []const u8,\n        description: ?[]const u8 = null,\n        priority: ?[]const u8 = null,\n    },\n    add: struct {\n        epic_id: []const u8,\n        issue_id: []const u8,\n    },\n    remove: struct {\n        epic_id: []const u8,\n        issue_id: []const u8,\n    },\n    list: struct {\n        epic_id: []const u8,\n    },\n};\n\n/// Epic command arguments.\npub const EpicArgs = struct {\n    subcommand: EpicSubcommand,\n};\n\n/// Dependency subcommand variants.\npub const DepSubcommand = union(enum) {\n    add: struct {\n        child: []const u8,\n        parent: []const u8,\n        dep_type: []const u8 = \"blocks\",\n    },\n    remove: struct {\n        child: []const u8,\n        parent: []const u8,\n    },\n    list: struct {\n        id: []const u8,\n    },\n    tree: struct {\n        id: []const u8,\n    },\n    cycles: void,\n};\n\n/// Dependency command arguments.\npub const DepArgs = struct {\n    subcommand: DepSubcommand,\n};\n\n/// Graph command output formats.\npub const GraphFormat = enum {\n    ascii,\n    dot,\n\n    pub fn fromString(s: []const u8) ?GraphFormat {\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"ascii\")) return .ascii;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"dot\")) return .dot;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"graphviz\")) return .dot;\n        return null;\n    }\n};\n\n/// Graph command arguments.\npub const GraphArgs = struct {\n    id: ?[]const u8 = null, // Optional: show graph for specific issue, otherwise show all\n    format: GraphFormat = .ascii,\n    depth: ?u32 = null, // Max depth for tree traversal\n};\n\n/// Label subcommand variants.\npub const LabelSubcommand = union(enum) {\n    add: struct {\n        id: []const u8,\n        labels: []const []const u8,\n    },\n    remove: struct {\n        id: []const u8,\n        labels: []const []const u8,\n    },\n    list: struct {\n        id: []const u8,\n    },\n    list_all: void,\n};\n\n/// Label command arguments.\npub const LabelArgs = struct {\n    subcommand: LabelSubcommand,\n};\n\n/// Comments subcommand variants.\npub const CommentsSubcommand = union(enum) {\n    add: struct {\n        id: []const u8,\n        text: []const u8,\n    },\n    list: struct {\n        id: []const u8,\n    },\n};\n\n/// Comments command arguments.\npub const CommentsArgs = struct {\n    subcommand: CommentsSubcommand,\n};\n\n/// History command arguments.\npub const HistoryArgs = struct {\n    id: []const u8,\n};\n\n/// Audit command arguments.\npub const AuditArgs = struct {\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n};\n\n/// Changelog command arguments.\npub const ChangelogArgs = struct {\n    since: ?[]const u8 = null, // Start date filter (YYYY-MM-DD)\n    until: ?[]const u8 = null, // End date filter (YYYY-MM-DD)\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n    group_by: ?[]const u8 = null, // Group by field (e.g., \"type\")\n};\n\n/// Sync command arguments.\npub const SyncArgs = struct {\n    flush_only: bool = false,\n    import_only: bool = false,\n};\n\n/// Shell completion types.\npub const Shell = enum {\n    bash,\n    zsh,\n    fish,\n    powershell,\n\n    pub fn fromString(s: []const u8) ?Shell {\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"bash\")) return .bash;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"zsh\")) return .zsh;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"fish\")) return .fish;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"powershell\")) return .powershell;\n        if (std.ascii.eqlIgnoreCase(s, \"ps\")) return .powershell;\n        return null;\n    }\n};\n\n/// Completions command arguments.\npub const CompletionsArgs = struct {\n    shell: Shell,\n};\n\n/// Help command arguments.\npub const HelpArgs = struct {\n    topic: ?[]const u8 = null,\n};\n\n/// Config subcommand variants.\npub const ConfigSubcommand = union(enum) {\n    get: struct {\n        key: []const u8,\n    },\n    set: struct {\n        key: []const u8,\n        value: []const u8,\n    },\n    list: void,\n};\n\n/// Config command arguments.\npub const ConfigArgs = struct {\n    subcommand: ConfigSubcommand,\n};\n\n/// Orphans command arguments.\npub const OrphansArgs = struct {\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n    hierarchy_only: bool = false,\n    deps_only: bool = false,\n};\n\n/// Lint command arguments.\npub const LintArgs = struct {\n    limit: ?u32 = null,\n};\n\n/// Result of parsing command-line arguments.\npub const ParseResult = struct {\n    global: GlobalOptions,\n    command: Command,\n\n    /// Free any memory allocated during parsing (labels, deps slices).\n    pub fn deinit(self: *ParseResult, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n        switch (self.command) {\n            .create => |create| {\n                if (create.labels.len > 0) allocator.free(create.labels);\n                if (create.deps.len > 0) allocator.free(create.deps);\n            },\n            .label => |label_cmd| {\n                switch (label_cmd.subcommand) {\n                    .add => |add| if (add.labels.len > 0) allocator.free(add.labels),\n                    .remove => |remove| if (remove.labels.len > 0) allocator.free(remove.labels),\n                    else => {},\n                }\n            },\n            else => {},\n        }\n    }\n};\n\n/// Errors that can occur during argument parsing.\npub const ParseError = error{\n    UnknownCommand,\n    MissingRequiredArgument,\n    InvalidArgument,\n    UnknownFlag,\n    MissingFlagValue,\n    InvalidFlagValue,\n    InvalidShell,\n    UnknownSubcommand,\n};\n\n/// Command-line argument parser.\npub const ArgParser = struct {\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    args: []const []const u8,\n    index: usize = 0,\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    pub fn init(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, args: []const []const u8) Self {\n        return .{\n            .allocator = allocator,\n            .args = args,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Parse all arguments into a ParseResult.\n    pub fn parse(self: *Self) ParseError!ParseResult {\n        var global = GlobalOptions{};\n\n        // Parse global flags first\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            const arg = self.peek().?;\n            if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, arg, \"-\")) {\n                if (self.parseGlobalFlag(&global)) |consumed| {\n                    if (!consumed) break;\n                } else |_| {\n                    break;\n                }\n            } else {\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Parse subcommand\n        const cmd_str = self.next() orelse {\n            return .{\n                .global = global,\n                .command = .{ .help = .{ .topic = null } },\n            };\n        };\n\n        const command = try self.parseCommand(cmd_str);\n\n        return .{\n            .global = global,\n            .command = command,\n        };\n    }\n\n    fn parseGlobalFlag(self: *Self, global: *GlobalOptions) ParseError!bool {\n        const arg = self.next().?;\n\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--json\")) {\n            global.json = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--toon\")) {\n            global.toon = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-q\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--quiet\")) {\n            global.quiet = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-v\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--verbose\")) {\n            global.verbose +|= 1;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"-vv\")) {\n            global.verbose +|= 2;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-color\")) {\n            global.no_color = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-auto-flush\")) {\n            global.no_auto_flush = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--no-auto-import\")) {\n            global.no_auto_import = true;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--data\") or std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--db\")) {\n            global.data_path = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--actor\")) {\n            global.actor = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            return true;\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, \"--lock-timeout\")) {\n            const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            global.lock_timeout = std.fmt.parseInt(u32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            return true;\n        }\n\n        // Put back if not recognized\n        self.index -= 1;\n        return error.UnknownFlag;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCommand(self: *Self, cmd: []const u8) ParseError!Command {\n        // Workspace\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"init\")) {\n            return .{ .init = try self.parseInitArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"info\")) {\n            return .{ .info = {} };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"stats\")) {\n            return .{ .stats = {} };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"doctor\")) {\n            return .{ .doctor = {} };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"config\")) {\n            return .{ .config = try self.parseConfigArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"orphans\")) {\n            return .{ .orphans = try self.parseOrphansArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"lint\")) {\n            return .{ .lint = try self.parseLintArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Issue CRUD\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"create\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"add\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"new\")) {\n            return .{ .create = try self.parseCreateArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"q\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"quick\")) {\n            return .{ .q = try self.parseQuickArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"show\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"get\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"view\")) {\n            return .{ .show = try self.parseShowArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"update\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"edit\")) {\n            return .{ .update = try self.parseUpdateArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"close\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"done\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"finish\")) {\n            return .{ .close = try self.parseCloseArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"reopen\")) {\n            return .{ .reopen = try self.parseReopenArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"delete\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"rm\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"remove\")) {\n            return .{ .delete = try self.parseDeleteArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Batch Operations\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"add-batch\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"batch-add\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"batch\")) {\n            return .{ .add_batch = try self.parseAddBatchArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"import\")) {\n            return .{ .import_cmd = try self.parseImportArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Query\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"list\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"ls\")) {\n            return .{ .list = try self.parseListArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"ready\")) {\n            return .{ .ready = try self.parseReadyArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"blocked\")) {\n            return .{ .blocked = try self.parseBlockedArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"search\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"find\")) {\n            return .{ .search = try self.parseSearchArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"stale\")) {\n            return .{ .stale = try self.parseStaleArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"count\")) {\n            return .{ .count = try self.parseCountArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"defer\")) {\n            return .{ .defer_cmd = try self.parseDeferArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"undefer\")) {\n            return .{ .undefer = try self.parseUndeferArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Dependencies\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"dep\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"deps\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"dependency\")) {\n            return .{ .dep = try self.parseDepArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"graph\")) {\n            return .{ .graph = try self.parseGraphArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Epics\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"epic\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"epics\")) {\n            return .{ .epic = try self.parseEpicArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Labels\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"label\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"labels\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"tag\")) {\n            return .{ .label = try self.parseLabelArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Comments\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"comments\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"comment\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"note\")) {\n            return .{ .comments = try self.parseCommentsArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Audit\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"history\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"log\")) {\n            return .{ .history = try self.parseHistoryArgs() };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"audit\")) {\n            return .{ .audit = try self.parseAuditArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Changelog\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"changelog\")) {\n            return .{ .changelog = try self.parseChangelogArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Sync\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"sync\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"flush\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"export\")) {\n            return .{ .sync = try self.parseSyncArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // System\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"version\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"--version\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"-V\")) {\n            return .{ .version = {} };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"schema\")) {\n            return .{ .schema = {} };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"completions\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"completion\")) {\n            return .{ .completions = try self.parseCompletionsArgs() };\n        }\n\n        // Help\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"help\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"--help\") or std.mem.eql(u8, cmd, \"-h\")) {\n            return .{ .help = try self.parseHelpArgs() };\n        }\n\n        return error.UnknownCommand;\n    }\n\n    fn parseInitArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!InitArgs {\n        var result = InitArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--prefix\")) {\n                result.prefix = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                result.prefix = self.next().?;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCreateArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!CreateArgs {\n        var result = CreateArgs{ .title = undefined };\n        var title_set = false;\n        var labels: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n        var deps: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-d\", \"--description\")) {\n                result.description = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-t\", \"--type\")) {\n                result.issue_type = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--priority\")) {\n                result.priority = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-a\", \"--assignee\")) {\n                result.assignee = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-l\", \"--label\")) {\n                labels.append(self.allocator, self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"--depends-on\", \"--dep\")) {\n                deps.append(self.allocator, self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(null, \"--due\")) {\n                result.due = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-e\", \"--estimate\")) {\n                const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n                result.estimate = std.fmt.parseInt(i32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!title_set) {\n                    result.title = self.next().?;\n                    title_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!title_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n\n        if (labels.items.len > 0) {\n            result.labels = labels.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n        }\n        if (deps.items.len > 0) {\n            result.deps = deps.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n        }\n\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseQuickArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!QuickArgs {\n        var result = QuickArgs{ .title = undefined };\n        var title_set = false;\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--priority\")) {\n                result.priority = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!title_set) {\n                    result.title = self.next().?;\n                    title_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!title_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseShowArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!ShowArgs {\n        var result = ShowArgs{ .id = undefined };\n        var id_set = false;\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(null, \"--no-comments\")) {\n                result.with_comments = false;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(null, \"--with-history\")) {\n                result.with_history = true;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!id_set) {\n                    result.id = self.next().?;\n                    id_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!id_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseUpdateArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!UpdateArgs {\n        var result = UpdateArgs{ .id = undefined };\n        var id_set = false;\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(null, \"--title\")) {\n                result.title = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-d\", \"--description\")) {\n                result.description = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-t\", \"--type\")) {\n                result.issue_type = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--priority\")) {\n                result.priority = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-a\", \"--assignee\")) {\n                result.assignee = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-s\", \"--status\")) {\n                result.status = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-v\", \"--version\")) {\n                const version_str = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n                result.expected_version = std.fmt.parseInt(u64, version_str, 10) catch return error.InvalidFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!id_set) {\n                    result.id = self.next().?;\n                    id_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!id_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCloseArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!CloseArgs {\n        var result = CloseArgs{ .id = undefined };\n        var id_set = false;\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-r\", \"--reason\")) {\n                result.reason = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!id_set) {\n                    result.id = self.next().?;\n                    id_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!id_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseReopenArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!ReopenArgs {\n        const id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return .{ .id = id };\n    }\n\n    fn parseDeleteArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!DeleteArgs {\n        const id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return .{ .id = id };\n    }\n\n    fn parseAddBatchArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!AddBatchArgs {\n        var result = AddBatchArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-f\", \"--file\")) {\n                result.file = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(null, \"--format\")) {\n                const fmt_str = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n                result.format = BatchFormat.fromString(fmt_str) orelse return error.InvalidArgument;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                // Positional argument is treated as file path\n                if (result.file == null) {\n                    result.file = self.next().?;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseImportArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!ImportArgs {\n        var result = ImportArgs{ .file = undefined };\n        var file_set = false;\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-m\", \"--merge\")) {\n                result.merge = true;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-n\", \"--dry-run\")) {\n                result.dry_run = true;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!file_set) {\n                    result.file = self.next().?;\n                    file_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!file_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseListArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!ListArgs {\n        var
