         } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--priority\")) {\n                result.priority = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-t\", \"--type\")) {\n                result.issue_type = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-a\", \"--assignee\")) {\n                result.assignee = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-l\", \"--label\")) {\n                result.label = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-A\", \"--all\")) {\n                result.all = true;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(null, \"--sort\")) {\n                const sort_str = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n                result.sort = SortField.fromString(sort_str) orelse return error.InvalidArgument;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(null, \"--asc\")) {\n                result.sort_desc = false;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(null, \"--desc\")) {\n                result.sort_desc = true;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseReadyArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!ReadyArgs {\n        var result = ReadyArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseBlockedArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!BlockedArgs {\n        var result = BlockedArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseSearchArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!SearchArgs {\n        var result = SearchArgs{ .query = undefined };\n        var query_set = false;\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (!query_set) {\n                    result.query = self.next().?;\n                    query_set = true;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        if (!query_set) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseStaleArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!StaleArgs {\n        var result = StaleArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-d\", \"--days\")) {\n                result.days = try self.consumeU32() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCountArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!CountArgs {\n        var result = CountArgs{};\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-g\", \"--group-by\")) {\n                result.group_by = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseDeferArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!DeferArgs {\n        const id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        var result = DeferArgs{ .id = id };\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-u\", \"--until\")) {\n                result.until = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-r\", \"--reason\")) {\n                result.reason = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseUndeferArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!UndeferArgs {\n        const id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n        return UndeferArgs{ .id = id };\n    }\n\n    fn parseDepArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!DepArgs {\n        const subcmd = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"add\")) {\n            const child = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            const parent = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            var dep_type: []const u8 = \"blocks\";\n            while (self.hasNext()) {\n                if (self.consumeFlag(\"-t\", \"--type\")) {\n                    dep_type = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n                } else break;\n            }\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .add = .{ .child = child, .parent = parent, .dep_type = dep_type } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"remove\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"rm\")) {\n            const child = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            const parent = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .remove = .{ .child = child, .parent = parent } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"list\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"ls\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list = .{ .id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"tree\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .tree = .{ .id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"cycles\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .cycles = {} } };\n        }\n        return error.UnknownSubcommand;\n    }\n\n    fn parseGraphArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!GraphArgs {\n        var result = GraphArgs{};\n\n        while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (self.consumeFlag(\"-f\", \"--format\")) {\n                const fmt_str = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n                result.format = GraphFormat.fromString(fmt_str) orelse return error.InvalidArgument;\n            } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-d\", \"--depth\")) {\n                result.depth = try self.consumeU32() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n            } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                if (result.id == null) {\n                    result.id = self.next().?;\n                } else break;\n            } else break;\n        }\n\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn parseEpicArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!EpicArgs {\n        const subcmd = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"create\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"new\")) {\n            var title: ?[]const u8 = null;\n            var description: ?[]const u8 = null;\n            var priority: ?[]const u8 = null;\n\n            while (self.hasNext()) {\n                if (self.consumeFlag(\"-d\", \"--description\")) {\n                    description = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n                } else if (self.consumeFlag(\"-p\", \"--priority\")) {\n                    priority = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n                } else if (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                    if (title == null) {\n                        title = self.next().?;\n                    } else break;\n                } else break;\n            }\n\n            if (title == null) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .create = .{\n                .title = title.?,\n                .description = description,\n                .priority = priority,\n            } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"add\")) {\n            const epic_id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            const issue_id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .add = .{ .epic_id = epic_id, .issue_id = issue_id } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"remove\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"rm\")) {\n            const epic_id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            const issue_id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .remove = .{ .epic_id = epic_id, .issue_id = issue_id } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"list\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"ls\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list = .{ .epic_id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument } } };\n        }\n        return error.UnknownSubcommand;\n    }\n\n    fn parseLabelArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!LabelArgs {\n        const subcmd = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"add\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"remove\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"rm\")) {\n            const is_add = std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"add\");\n            const id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n            var labels: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n\n            while (self.peekPositional()) |_| {\n                labels.append(self.allocator, self.next().?) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            }\n\n            if (labels.items.len == 0) return error.MissingRequiredArgument;\n\n            const label_slice = labels.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n            if (is_add) {\n                return .{ .subcommand = .{ .add = .{ .id = id, .labels = label_slice } } };\n            } else {\n                return .{ .subcommand = .{ .remove = .{ .id = id, .labels = label_slice } } };\n            }\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"list\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"ls\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list = .{ .id = self.next() orelse return error.MissingRequiredArgument } } };\n        }\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"list-all\") or std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"all\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list_all = {} } };\n        }\n        return error.UnknownSubcommand;\n    }\n\n    fn parseCommentsArgs(self: *Self) ParseError!CommentsArgs {\n        const subcmd = self.next() orelse return orelse return .{ .subcommand = .{ .list = {} } };\n\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, subcmd, \"get\")) {\n            return .{ .subcommand = .{ .get = .{ .key = self.next() orelse return while (self.hasNext()) {\n            if (try self.parseLimitFlag()) |limit| {\n                result.limit = limit;\n            } else break;\n        }\n        return result;\n    }\n\n    fn hasNext(self: *Self) bool {\n        return self.index < self.args.len;\n    }\n\n    fn peek(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n        return self.args[self.index];\n    }\n\n    fn next(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n        if (self.index >= self.args.len) return null;\n        const arg = self.args[self.index];\n        self.index += 1;\n        return arg;\n    }\n\n    /// Skip a peeked argument (used after checking with peek() and wanting to consume it).\n    fn skip(self: *Self) void {\n        if (self.index < self.args.len) {\n            self.index += 1;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Check if current arg matches a flag, and if so consume it and return true.\n    fn consumeFlag(self: *Self, short: ?[]const u8, long: []const u8) bool {\n        const arg = self.peek() orelse return false;\n        if (std.mem.eql(u8, arg, long) or (short != null and std.mem.eql(u8, arg, short.?))) {\n            self.skip();\n            return true;\n        }\n        return false;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse a u32 value after consuming a flag. Returns null if missing, error if invalid.\n    fn consumeU32(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n        const val = self.next() orelse return error.MissingFlagValue;\n        return std.fmt.parseInt(u32, val, 10) catch return error.InvalidArgument;\n    }\n\n    /// Parse an optional --limit/-n flag, returning the value if present.\n    fn parseLimitFlag(self: *Self) ParseError!?u32 {\n        if (self.consumeFlag(\"-n\", \"--limit\")) {\n            return try self.consumeU32();\n        }\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    /// Returns the next arg if it's a positional (doesn't start with \"-\"), otherwise null.\n    fn peekPositional(self: *Self) ?[]const u8 {\n        const arg = self.peek() orelse return null;\n        if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, arg, \"-\")) return null;\n        return arg;\n    }\n};\n\n// Tests\n\ntest \"parse no arguments shows help\" {\n    const args = [_][]const u8{};\n    var parser = ArgParser.init(std.testing.allocator, mode\n    const json_opts = GlobalOptions{ .json = true };\n    try std.testing.expect(json_opts.isStructuredOutput());\n\n    // TOON mode\n    const toon_opts = GlobalOptions{ .toon = true };\n self.dirty_ids.keyIterator();\n    80→        while (dirty_it.next()) |key| {\n    81→            self.allocator.free(key.*);\n    82→        }\n    83→        self.dirty_ids.deinit(self.allocator);\n    84→    }\n    85→\n    86→    /// Load issues from the JSONL file into memory.\n    87→    pub fn loadFromFile(self: *Self) !void {\n    88→        var jsonl = JsonlFile.init(self.jsonl_path, self.allocator);\n    89→        const loaded_issues = try jsonl.readAll();\n    90→        defer self.allocator.free(loaded_issues);\n    91→\n    92→        for (loaded_issues) |issue| {\n    93→            const id_copy = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, issue.id);\n    94→            errdefer self.allocator.free(id_copy);\n    95→\n    96→            const idx = self.issues.items.len;\n    97→            try self.issues.append(self.allocator, issue);\n    98→            try self.id_index.put(self.allocator, id_copy, idx);\n    99→        }\n   100→\n   101→        self.dirty = false;\n   102→    }\n   103→\n   104→    /// Load issues from the JSONL file with graceful corruption recovery.\n   105→    /// Logs and skips corrupt entries instead of failing.\n   106→    /// Returns statistics about the load including corruption count.\n   107→    pub fn loadFromFileWithRecovery(self: *Self) !StoreLoadResult {\n   108→        var jsonl = JsonlFile.init(self.jsonl_path, self.allocator);\n   109→        var load_result = try jsonl.readAllWithRecovery();\n   110→        // Take ownership of corrupt_lines before freeing issues slice\n   111→        const corrupt_lines = load_result.corrupt_lines;\n   112→        load_result.corrupt_lines = &.{}; // Prevent double-free\n   113→        errdefer if (corrupt_lines.len > 0) self.allocator.free(corrupt_lines);\n   114→\n   115→        const loaded_issues = load_result.issues;\n   116→        defer self.allocator.free(loaded_issues);\n   117→\n   118→        for (loaded_issues) |issue| {\n   119→            const id_copy = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, issue.id);\n   120→            errdefer self.allocator.free(id_copy);\n   121→\n   122→            const idx = self.issues.items.len;\n   123→            try self.issues.append(self.allocator, issue);\n   124→            try self.id_index.put(self.allocator, id_copy, idx);\n   125→        }\n   126→\n   127→        self.dirty = false;\n   128→\n   129→        return StoreLoadResult{\n   130→            .jsonl_corruption_count = load_result.corruption_count,\n   131→            .jsonl_corrupt_lines = corrupt_lines,\n   132→        };\n   133→    }\n   134→\n   135→    /// Save all issues to the JSONL file.\n   136→    pub fn saveToFile(self: *Self) !void {\n   137→        var jsonl = JsonlFile.init(self.jsonl_path, self.allocator);\n   138→        try jsonl.writeAll(self.issues.items);\n   139→        self.dirty = false;\n   140→\n   141→        // Clear dirty tracking\n   142→        var dirty_it = self.dirty_ids.keyIterator();\n   143→        while (dirty_it.next()) |key| {\n   144→            self.allocator.free(key.*);\n   145→        }\n   146→        self.dirty_ids.clearRetainingCapacity();\n   147→    }\n   148→\n   149→    /// Insert a new issue into the store.\n   150→    pub fn insert(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n   151→        if (self.id_index.contains(issue.id)) {\n   152→            return IssueStoreError.DuplicateId;\n   153→        }\n   154→\n   155→        const cloned = try issue.clone(self.allocator);\n   156→        errdefer {\n   157→            var c = cloned;\n   158→            c.deinit(self.allocator);\n   159→        }\n   160→\n   161→        const id_copy = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, cloned.id);\n   162→        errdefer self.allocator.free(id_copy);\n   163→\n   164→        const idx = self.issues.items.len;\n   165→        try self.issues.append(self.allocator, cloned);\n   166→        try self.id_index.put(self.allocator, id_copy, idx);\n   167→\n   168→        try self.markDirty(issue.id);\n   169→    }\n   170→\n   171→    /// Get an issue by ID (without embedded relations).\n   172→    pub fn get(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !?Issue {\n   173→        const idx = self.id_index.get(id) orelse return null;\n   174→        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return null;\n   175→\n   176→        return try self.issues.items[idx].clone(self.allocator);\n   177→    }\n   178→\n   179→    /// Get an issue with all embedded relations (labels, deps, comments).\n   180→    /// Since we store everything in-memory, this just returns the issue as-is.\n   181→    pub fn getWithRelations(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !?Issue {\n   182→        return try self.get(id);\n   183→    }\n   184→\n   185→    /// Get a reference to the stored issue (no clone).\n   186→    /// Caller must NOT free or modify the returned issue.\n   187→    pub fn getRef(self: *Self, id: []const u8) ?*Issue {\n   188→        const idx = self.id_index.get(id) orelse return null;\n   189→        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return null;\n   190→        return &self.issues.items[idx];\n   191→    }\n   192→\n   193→    /// Fields that can be updated on an issue.\n   194→    pub const IssueUpdate = struct {\n   195→        title: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   196→        description: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   197→        design: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   198→        acceptance_criteria: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   199→        notes: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   200→        status: ?Status = null,\n   201→        priority: ?Priority = null,\n   202→        issue_type: ?IssueType = null,\n   203→        assignee: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   204→        owner: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   205→        estimated_minutes: ?i32 = null,\n   206→        closed_at: ?i64 = null,\n   207→        close_reason: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   208→        due_at: ?i64 = null,\n   209→        defer_until: ?i64 = null,\n   210→        external_ref: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   211→        source_system: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   212→        pinned: ?bool = null,\n   213→        is_template: ?bool = null,\n   214→        content_hash: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   215→\n   216→        /// Expected version for optimistic locking.\n   217→        /// If set, update will fail with VersionMismatch if issue.version != expected_version.\n   218→        expected_version: ?u64 = null,\n   219→    };\n   220→\n   221→    /// Update an issue with the given fields.\n   222→    /// If updates.expected_version is set, performs optimistic locking check.\n   223→    pub fn update(self: *Self, id: []const u8, updates: IssueUpdate, now: i64) !void {\n   224→        const idx = self.id_index.get(id) orelse return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n   225→        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n   226→\n   227→        var issue = &self.issues.items[idx];\n   228→\n   229→        // Optimistic locking check\n   230→        if (updates.expected_version) |expected| {\n   231→            if (issue.version != expected) {\n   232→                return IssueStoreError.VersionMismatch;\n   233→            }\n   234→        }\n   235→\n   236→        // Increment version on every update\n   237→        issue.version += 1;\n   238→\n   239→        // Update timestamp\n   240→        issue.updated_at = Rfc3339Timestamp{ .value = now };\n   241→\n   242→        // Apply updates\n   243→        if (updates.title) |v| {\n   244→            self.allocator.free(issue.title);\n   245→            issue.title = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n   246→        }\n   247→        if (updates.description) |v| {\n   248→            if (issue.description) |d| self.allocator.free(d);\n   249→            issue.description = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n   250→        }\n   251→        if (updates.design) |v| {\n   252→            if (issue.design) |d| self.allocator.free(d);\n   253→            issue.design = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n   254→        }\n   255→        if (updates.acceptance_criteria) |v| {\n   256→            if (issue.acceptance_criteria) |a| self.allocator.free(a);\n   257→            issue.acceptance_criteria = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n   258→        }\n   259→        if (updates.notes) |v| {\n   260→            if (issue.notes) |n| self.allocator.free(n);\n   261→            issue.notes = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n   262→        }\n   263→        if (updates.status) |v| {\n   264→            freeStatus(issue.status, self.allocator);\n   265→            issue.status = try cloneStatus(v, self.allocator);\n   266→        }\n   267→        if (updates.priority) |v| {\n   268→            issue.priority = v;\n   269→        }\n   270→        if (updates.issue_type) |v| {\n   271→            freeIssueType(issue.issue_type, self.allocator);\n   272→            issue.issue_type = try cloneIssueType(v, self.allocator);\n   273→        }\n   274→        if (updates.assignee) |v| {\n   275→            if (issue.assignee) |a| self.allocator.free(a);\n   276→            issue.assignee = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n   277→        }\n   278→        if (updates.owner) |v| {\n   279→            if (issue.owner) |o| self.allocator.free(o);\n   280→            issue.owner = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n   281→        }\n   282→        if (updates.estimated_minutes) |v| {\n   283→            issue.estimated_minutes = v;\n   284→        }\n   285→        if (updates.closed_at) |v| {\n   286→            issue.closed_at = OptionalRfc3339Timestamp{ .value = v };\n   287→        }\n   288→        if (updates.close_reason) |v| {\n   289→            if (issue.close_reason) |r| self.allocator.free(r);\n   290→            issue.close_reason = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n   291→        }\n   292→        if (updates.due_at) |v| {\n   293→            issue.due_at = OptionalRfc3339Timestamp{ .value = v };\n   294→        }\n   295→        if (updates.defer_until) |v| {\n   296→            issue.defer_until = OptionalRfc3339Timestamp{ .value = v };\n   297→        }\n   298→        if (updates.external_ref) |v| {\n   299→            if (issue.external_ref) |e| self.allocator.free(e);\n   300→            issue.external_ref = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n   301→        }\n   302→        if (updates.source_system) |v| {\n   303→            if (issue.source_system) |s| self.allocator.free(s);\n   304→            issue.source_system = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n   305→        }\n   306→        if (updates.pinned) |v| {\n   307→            issue.pinned = v;\n   308→        }\n   309→        if (updates.is_template) |v| {\n   310→            issue.is_template = v;\n   311→        }\n   312→        if (updates.content_hash) |v| {\n   313→            if (issue.content_hash) |h| self.allocator.free(h);\n   314→            issue.content_hash = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n   315→        }\n   316→\n   317→        try self.markDirty(id);\n   318→    }\n   319→\n   320→    /// Soft delete an issue by setting its status to tombstone.\n   321→    pub fn delete(self: *Self, id: []const u8, now: i64) !void {\n   322→        try self.update(id, .{ .status = .tombstone }, now);\n   323→    }\n   324→\n   325→    /// Filters for listing issues.\n   326→    pub const ListFilters = struct {\n   327→        status: ?Status = null,\n   328→        priority: ?Priority = null,\n   329→        issue_type: ?IssueType = null,\n   330→        assignee: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   331→        label: ?[]const u8 = null,\n   332→        include_tombstones: bool = false,\n   333→        limit: ?u32 = null,\n   334→        offset: ?u32 = null,\n   335→        order_by: OrderBy = .created_at,\n   336→        order_desc: bool = true,\n   337→\n   338→        pub const OrderBy = enum {\n   339→            created_at,\n   340→            updated_at,\n   341→            priority,\n   342→        };\n   343→    };\n   344→\n   345→    /// List issues with optional filters.\n   346→    pub fn list(self: *Self, filters: ListFilters) ![]Issue {\n   347→        var results: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(Issue) = .{};\n   348→        errdefer {\n   349→            for (results.items) |*issue| {\n   350→                issue.deinit(self.allocator);\n   351→            }\n   352→            results.deinit(self.allocator);\n   353→        }\n   354→\n   355→        for (self.issues.items) |issue| {\n   356→            // Filter tombstones\n   357→            if (!filters.include_tombstones and statusEql(issue.status, .tombstone)) {\n   358→                continue;\n   359→            }\n   360→\n   361→            // Apply filters\n   362→            if (filters.status) |s| {\n   363→                if (!statusEql(issue.status, s)) continue;\n   364→            }\n   365→            if (filters.priority) |p| {\n   366→                if (issue.priority.value != p.value) continue;\n   367→            }\n   368→            if (filters.issue_type) |t| {\n   369→                if (!issueTypeEql(issue.issue_type, t)) continue;\n   370→            }\n   371→            if (filters.assignee) |a| {\n   372→                if (issue.assignee == null) continue;\n   373→                if (!std.mem.eql(u8, issue.assignee.?, a)) continue;\n   374→            }\n   375→            if (filters.label) |lbl| {\n   376→                var found = false;\n   377→                for (issue.labels) |label| {\n   378→                    if (std.mem.eql(u8, label, lbl)) {\n   379→                        found = true;\n   380→                        break;\n   381→                    }\n   382→                }\n   383→                if (!found) continue;\n   384→            }\n   385→\n   386→            try results.append(self.allocator, try issue.clone(self.allocator));\n   387→        }\n   388→\n   389→        // Sort\n   390→        const SortContext = struct {\n   391→            order_by: ListFilters.OrderBy,\n   392→            order_desc: bool,\n   393→        };\n   394→        const ctx = SortContext{ .order_by = filters.order_by, .order_desc = filters.order_desc };\n   395→\n   396→        std.mem.sortUnstable(Issue, results.items, ctx, struct {\n   397→            fn lessThan(c: SortContext, a: Issue, b: Issue) bool {\n   398→                const cmp: i64 = switch (c.order_by) {\n   399→                    .created_at => a.created_at.value - b.created_at.value,\n   400→                    .updated_at => a.updated_at.value - b.updated_at.value,\n   401→                    .priority => @as(i64, a.priority.value) - @as(i64, b.priority.value),\n   402→                };\n   403→                return if (c.order_desc) cmp > 0 else cmp < 0;\n   404→            }\n   405→        }.lessThan);\n   406→\n   407→        // Apply offset and limit\n   408→        var start: usize = 0;\n   409→        if (filters.offset) |off| {\n   410→            start = @min(off, results.items.len);\n   411→        }\n   412→\n   413→        var end: usize = results.items.len;\n   414→        if (filters.limit) |lim| {\n   415→            end = @min(start + lim, results.items.len);\n   416→        }\n   417→\n   418→        // Free items outside the range\n   419→        for (results.items[0..start]) |*issue| {\n   420→            issue.deinit(self.allocator);\n   421→        }\n   422→        for (results.items[end..]) |*issue| {\n   423→            issue.deinit(self.allocator);\n   424→        }\n   425→\n   426→        // Return slice\n   427→        const slice = try self.allocator.dupe(Issue, results.items[start..end]);\n   428→        results.deinit(self.allocator);\n   429→        return slice;\n   430→    }\n   431→\n   432→    /// Result from counting issues.\n   433→    pub const CountResult = struct {\n   434→        key: []const u8,\n   435→        count: u64,\n   436→    };\n   437→\n   438→    /// Count issues, optionally grouped by a field.\n   439→    pub fn count(self: *Self, group_by: ?GroupBy) ![]CountResult {\n   440→        var counts: std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(u64) = .{};\n   441→        defer counts.deinit(self.allocator);\n   442→\n   443→        for (self.issues.items) |issue| {\n   444→            if (statusEql(issue.status, .tombstone)) continue;\n   445→\n   446→            const key_str: []const u8 = if (group_by) |g| switch (g) {\n   447→                .status => issue.status.toString(),\n   448→                .priority => switch (issue.priority.value) {\n   449→                    0 => \"0\",\n   450→                    1 => \"1\",\n   451→                    2 => \"2\",\n   452→                    3 => \"3\",\n   453→                    4 => \"4\",\n   454→                    else => unreachable,\n   455→                },\n   456→                .issue_type => issue.issue_type.toString(),\n   457→                .assignee => issue.assignee orelse \"(unassigned)\",\n   458→            } else \"total\";\n   459→\n   460→            const entry = counts.getOrPutValue(self.allocator, key_str, 0) catch continue;\n   461→            entry.value_ptr.* += 1;\n   462→        }\n   463→\n   464→        var results: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(CountResult) = .{};\n   465→        errdefer {\n   466→            for (results.items) |r| {\n   467→                self.allocator.free(r.key);\n   468→            }\n   469→            results.deinit(self.allocator);\n   470→        }\n   471→\n   472→        var it = counts.iterator();\n   473→        while (it.next()) |entry| {\n   474→            const key = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, entry.key_ptr.*);\n   475→            try results.append(self.allocator, .{ .key = key, .count = entry.value_ptr.* });\n   476→        }\n   477→\n   478→        return results.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator);\n   479→    }\n   480→\n   481→    pub const GroupBy = enum {\n   482→        status,\n   483→        priority,\n   484→        issue_type,\n   485→        assignee,\n   486→    };\n   487→\n   488→    /// Check if an issue exists.\n   489→    pub fn exists(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !bool {\n   490→        return self.id_index.contains(id);\n   491→    }\n   492→\n   493→    /// Get labels for an issue.\n   494→    pub fn getLabels(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8) ![]const []const u8 {\n   495→        const idx = self.id_index.get(issue_id) orelse return &[_][]const u8{};\n   496→        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return &[_][]const u8{};\n   497→\n   498→        const issue = self.issues.items[idx];\n   499→        if (issue.labels.len == 0) return &[_][]const u8{};\n   500→\n   501→        const labels = try self.allocator.alloc([]const u8, issue.labels.len);\n   502→        errdefer self.allocator.free(labels);\n   503→\n   504→        for (issue.labels, 0..) |label, i| {\n   505→            labels[i] = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, label);\n   506→        }\n   507→        return labels;\n   508→    }\n   509→\n   510→    /// Add a label to an issue.\n   511→    pub fn addLabel(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8, label: []const u8) !void {\n   512→        const idx = self.id_index.get(issue_id) orelse return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n   513→        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n   514→\n   515→        var issue = &self.issues.items[idx];\n   516→\n   517→        // Check if already exists\n   518→        for (issue.labels) |existing| {\n   519→            if (std.mem.eql(u8, existing, label)) return;\n   520→        }\n   521→\n   522→        // Add new label\n   523→        const label_copy = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, label);\n   524→        errdefer self.allocator.free(label_copy);\n   525→\n   526→        const new_labels = try self.allocator.alloc([]const u8, issue.labels.len + 1);\n   527→        @memcpy(new_labels[0..issue.labels.len], issue.labels);\n   528→        new_labels[issue.labels.len] = label_copy;\n   529→\n   530→        if (issue.labels.len > 0) {\n   531→            self.allocator.free(issue.labels);\n   532→        }\n   533→        issue.labels = new_labels;\n   534→\n   535→        try self.markDirty(issue_id);\n   536→    }\n   537→\n   538→    /// Remove a label from an issue.\n   539→    pub fn removeLabel(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8, label: []const u8) !void {\n   540→        const idx = self.id_index.get(issue_id) orelse return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n   541→        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n   542→\n   543→        var issue = &self.issues.items[idx];\n   544→\n   545→        var found_idx: ?usize = null;\n   546→        for (issue.labels, 0..) |existing, i| {\n   547→            if (std.mem.eql(u8, existing, label)) {\n   548→                found_idx = i;\n   549→                break;\n   550→            }\n   551→        }\n   552→\n   553→        if (found_idx) |fi| {\n   554→            self.allocator.free(issue.labels[fi]);\n   555→\n   556→            if (issue.labels.len == 1) {\n   557→                self.allocator.free(issue.labels);\n   558→                issue.labels = &[_][]const u8{};\n   559→            } else {\n   560→                const new_labels = try self.allocator.alloc([]const u8, issue.labels.len - 1);\n   561→                var j: usize = 0;\n   562→                for (issue.labels, 0..) |lbl, i| {\n   563→                    if (i != fi) {\n   564→                        new_labels[j] = lbl;\n   565→                        j += 1;\n   566→                    }\n   567→                }\n   568→                self.allocator.free(issue.labels);\n   569→                issue.labels = new_labels;\n   570→            }\n   571→\n   572→            try self.markDirty(issue_id);\n   573→        }\n   574→    }\n   575→\n   576→    /// Get dependencies for an issue.\n   577→    pub fn getDependencies(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8) ![]const Dependency {\n   578→        const idx = self.id_index.get(issue_id) orelse return &[_]Dependency{};\n   579→        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return &[_]Dependency{};\n   580→\n   581→        const issue = self.issues.items[idx];\n   582→        if (issue.dependencies.len == 0) return &[_]Dependency{};\n   583→\n   584→        const deps = try self.allocator.alloc(Dependency, issue.dependencies.len);\n   585→        errdefer self.allocator.free(deps);\n   586→\n   587→        for (issue.dependencies, 0..) |dep, i| {\n   588→            deps[i] = try cloneDependency(dep, self.allocator);\n   589→        }\n   590→        return deps;\n   591→    }\n   592→\n   593→    /// Get comments for an issue.\n   594→    pub fn getComments(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8) ![]const Comment {\n   595→        const idx = self.id_index.get(issue_id) orelse return &[_]Comment{};\n   596→        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return &[_]Comment{};\n   597→\n   598→        const issue = self.issues.items[idx];\n   599→        if (issue.comments.len == 0) return &[_]Comment{};\n   600→\n   601→        const comments = try self.allocator.alloc(Comment, issue.comments.len);\n   602→        errdefer self.allocator.free(comments);\n   603→\n   604→        for (issue.comments, 0..) |c, i| {\n   605→            comments[i] = try cloneComment(c, self.allocator);\n   606→        }\n   607→        return comments;\n   608→    }\n   609→\n   610→    /// Add a comment to an issue.\n   611→    pub fn addComment(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8, comment: Comment) !void {\n   612→        const idx = self.id_index.get(issue_id) orelse return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n   613→        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n   614→\n   615→        var issue = &self.issues.items[idx];\n   616→\n   617→        const cloned = try cloneComment(comment, self.allocator);\n   618→        errdefer freeComment(@constCast(&cloned), self.allocator);\n   619→\n   620→        const new_comments = try self.allocator.alloc(Comment, issue.comments.len + 1);\n   621→        @memcpy(new_comments[0..issue.comments.len], issue.comments);\n   622→        new_comments[issue.comments.len] = cloned;\n   623→\n   624→        if (issue.comments.len > 0) {\n   625→            self.allocator.free(issue.comments);\n   626→        }\n   627→        issue.comments = new_comments;\n   628→\n   629→        try self.markDirty(issue_id);\n   630→    }\n   631→\n   632→    /// Mark an issue as dirty for sync.\n   633→    pub fn markDirty(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n   634→        self.dirty = true;\n   635→        const now = std.time.timestamp();\n   636→\n   637→        if (!self.dirty_ids.contains(id)) {\n   638→            const id_copy = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, id);\n   639→            try self.dirty_ids.put(self.allocator, id_copy, now);\n   640→        } else {\n   641→            self.dirty_ids.getPtr(id).?.* = now;\n   642→        }\n   643→    }\n   644→\n   645→    /// Clear dirty flag for an issue.\n   646→    pub fn clearDirty(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n   647→        if (self.dirty_ids.fetchRemove(id)) |kv| {\n   648→            self.allocator.free(kv.key);\n   649→        }\n   650→    }\n   651→\n   652→    /// Get all dirty issue IDs.\n   653→    pub fn getDirtyIds(self: *Self) ![][]const u8 {\n   654→        var ids: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n   655→        errdefer {\n   656→            for (ids.items) |id| {\n   657→                self.allocator.free(id);\n   658→            }\n   659→            ids.deinit(self.allocator);\n   660→        }\n   661→\n   662→        var it = self.dirty_ids.keyIterator();\n   663→        while (it.next()) |key| {\n   664→            const id = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, key.*);\n   665→            try ids.append(self.allocator, id);\n   666→        }\n   667→\n   668→        return ids.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator);\n   669→    }\n   670→\n   671→    /// Check if the store has unsaved changes.\n   672→    pub fn isDirty(self: *Self) bool {\n   673→        return self.dirty;\n   674→    }\n   675→\n   676→    /// Get total number of issues (excluding tombstones).\n   677→    pub fn countTotal(self: *Self) usize {\n   678→        var total: usize = 0;\n   679→        for (self.issues.items) |issue| {\n   680→            if (!statusEql(issue.status, .tombstone)) {\n   681→                total += 1;\n   682→            }\n   683→        }\n   684→        return total;\n   685→    }\n   686→\n   687→    /// Get all issues as a slice (no clone, read-only).\n   688→    pub fn getAllRef(self: *Self) []const Issue {\n   689→        return self.issues.items;\n   690→    }\n   691→\n   692→    /// Suggestion for similar ID lookup.\n   693→    pub const IdSuggestion = struct {\n   694→        id: []const u8,\n   695→        title: []const u8,\n   696→    };\n   697→\n   698→    /// Find similar IDs when a lookup fails (for \"did you mean\" suggestions).\n   699→    /// Uses prefix matching and Levenshtein-like scoring.\n   700→    /// Returns up to `max_count` suggestions, caller must free.\n   701→    pub fn findSimilarIds(self: *Self, target: []const u8, max_count: usize) ![]IdSuggestion {\n   702→        if (self.issues.items.len == 0) return &[_]IdSuggestion{};\n   703→\n   704→        const Scored = struct {\n   705→            id: []const u8,\n   706→            title: []const u8,\n   707→            score: i32,\n   708→        };\n   709→\n   710→        var candidates: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(Scored) = .{};\n   711→        defer candidates.deinit(self.allocator);\n   712→\n   713→        for (self.issues.items) |issue| {\n   714→            if (statusEql(issue.status, .tombstone)) continue;\n   715→\n   716→            const score = computeSimilarity(target, issue.id);\n   717→            if (score > 0) {\n   718→                try candidates.append(self.allocator, .{\n   719→                    .id = issue.id,\n   720→                    .title = issue.title,\n   721→                    .score = score,\n   722→                });\n   723→            }\n   724→        }\n   725→\n   726→        if (candidates.items.len == 0) return &[_]IdSuggestion{};\n   727→\n   728→        // Sort by score descending\n   729→        std.mem.sortUnstable(Scored, candidates.items, {}, struct {\n   730→            fn lessThan(_: void, a: Scored, b: Scored) bool {\n   731→                return a.score > b.score;\n   732→            }\n   733→        }.lessThan);\n   734→\n   735→        const result_count = @min(max_count, candidates.items.len);\n   736→        var suggestions = try self.allocator.alloc(IdSuggestion, result_count);\n   737→        errdefer self.allocator.free(suggestions);\n   738→\n   739→        for (0..result_count) |i| {\n   740→            suggestions[i] = .{\n   741→                .id = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, candidates.items[i].id),\n   742→                .title = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, candidates.items[i].title),\n   743→            };\n   744→        }\n   745→\n   746→        return suggestions;\n   747→    }\n   748→\n   749→    /// Free suggestions returned by findSimilarIds.\n   750→    pub fn freeSuggestions(self: *Self, suggestions: []IdSuggestion) void {\n   751→        for (suggestions) |s| {\n   752→            self.allocator.free(s.id);\n   753→            self.allocator.free(s.title);\n   754→        }\n   755→        self.allocator.free(suggestions);\n   756→    }\n   757→};\n   758→\n   759→/// Compute similarity score between target and candidate ID.\n   760→/// Higher score = more similar.\n   761→fn computeSimilarity(target: []const u8, candidate: []const u8) i32 {\n   762→    var score: i32 = 0;\n   763→\n   764→    // Exact prefix match (bd-abc matches bd-abc123)\n   765→    if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, candidate, target)) {\n   766→        score += 100;\n   767→    }\n   768→    // Candidate is prefix of target (bd-abc123 starts with bd-abc)\n   769→    else if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, target, candidate)) {\n   770→        score += 80;\n   771→    }\n   772→\n   773→    // Common prefix length\n   774→    var common_prefix: usize = 0;\n   775→    const min_len = @min(target.len, candidate.len);\n   776→    for (0..min_len) |i| {\n   777→        if (target[i] == candidate[i]) {\n   778→            common_prefix += 1;\n   779→        } else {\n   780→            break;\n   781→        }\n   782→    }\n   783→    score += @intCast(common_prefix * 5);\n   784→\n   785→    // Contains target as substring\n   786→    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, candidate, target) != null) {\n   787→        score += 30;\n   788→    }\n   789→\n   790→    // Similar length bonus\n   791→    const len_diff: i32 = @intCast(@abs(@as(i64, @intCast(target.len)) - @as(i64, @intCast(candidate.len))));\n   792→    if (len_diff <= 2) {\n   793→        score += 10;\n   794→    }\n   795→\n   796→    return score;\n   797→}\n   798→\n   799→// Helper functions\n   800→fn statusEql(a: Status, b: Status) bool {\n   801→    const Tag = std.meta.Tag(Status);\n   802→    const tag_a: Tag = a;\n   803→    const tag_b: Tag = b;\n   804→    if (tag_a != tag_b) return false;\n   805→    return if (tag_a == .custom) std.mem.eql(u8, a.custom, b.custom) else true;\n   806→}\n   807→\n   808→fn issueTypeEql(a: IssueType, b: IssueType) bool {\n   809→    const Tag = std.meta.Tag(IssueType);\n   810→    const tag_a: Tag = a;\n   811→    const tag_b: Tag = b;\n   812→    if (tag_a != tag_b) return false;\n   813→    return if (tag_a == .custom) std.mem.eql(u8, a.custom, b.custom) else true;\n   814→}\n   815→\n   816→fn cloneStatus(status: Status, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !Status {\n   817→    return switch (status) {\n   818→        .custom => |s| Status{ .custom = try allocator.dupe(u8, s) },\n   819→        else => status,\n   820→    };\n   821→}\n   822→\n   823→fn freeStatus(status: Status, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n   824→    switch (status) {\n   825→        .custom => |s| allocator.free(s),\n   826→        else => {},\n   827→    }\n   828→}\n   829→\n   830→fn cloneIssueType(issue_type: IssueType, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !IssueType {\n   831→    return switch (issue_type) {\n   832→        .custom => |s| IssueType{ .custom = try allocator.dupe(u8, s) },\n   833→        else => issue_type,\n   834→    };\n   835→}\n   836→\n   837→fn freeIssueType(issue_type: IssueType, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n   838→    switch (issue_type) {\n   839→        .custom => |s| allocator.free(s),\n   840→        else => {},\n   841→    }\n   842→}\n   843→\n   844→fn cloneDependency(dep: Dependency, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !Dependency {\n   845→    var result: Dependency = undefined;\n   846→\n   847→    result.issue_id = try allocator.dupe(u8, dep.issue_id);\n   848→    errdefer allocator.free(result.issue_id);\n   849→\n   850→    result.depends_on_id = try allocator.dupe(u8, dep.depends_on_id);\n   851→    errdefer allocator.free(result.depends_on_id);\n   852→\n   853→    result.dep_type = switch (dep.dep_type) {\n   854→        .custom => |s| .{ .custom = try allocator.dupe(u8, s) },\n   855→        else => dep.dep_type,\n   856→    };\n   857→\n   858→    result.created_at = dep.created_at;\n   859→    result.created_by = if (dep.created_by) |c| try allocator.dupe(u8, c) else null;\n   860→    result.metadata = if (dep.metadata) |m| try allocator.dupe(u8, m) else null;\n   861→    result.thread_id = if (dep.thread_id) |t| try allocator.dupe(u8, t) else null;\n   862→\n   863→    return result;\n   864→}\n   865→\n   866→fn cloneComment(comment: Comment, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !Comment {\n   867→    return Comment{\n   868→        .id = comment.id,\n   869→        .issue_id = try allocator.dupe(u8, comment.issue_id),\n   870→        .author = try allocator.dupe(u8, comment.author),\n   871→        .body = try allocator.dupe(u8, comment.body),\n   872→        .created_at = comment.created_at,\n   873→    };\n   874→}\n   875→\n   876→fn freeComment(comment: *Comment, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n   877→    allocator.free(comment.issue_id);\n   878→    allocator.free(comment.author);\n   879→    allocator.free(comment.body);\n   880→}\n   881→\n   882→// --- Tests ---\n   883→\n   884→test \"IssueStore insert and get\" {\n   885→    const allocator In-memory issue store for beads_zig.\n//!\n//! Provides CRUD operations for issues using in-memory storage with:\n//! - Arena allocator for issue memory management\n//! - ArrayList + StringHashMap for fast ID lookup\n//! - Dirty tracking for sync operations\n//! - JSONL persistence via JsonlFile\n\nconst std = @import(\"std\");\nconst JsonlFile = @import(\"jsonl.zig\").JsonlFile;\nconst Issue = @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Issue;\nconst Rfc3339Timestamp = @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").Rfc3339Timestamp;\nconst OptionalRfc3339Timestamp = @import(\"../models/issue.zig\").OptionalRfc3339Timestamp;\nconst Status = @import(\"../models/status.zig\").Status;\nconst Priority = @import(\"../models/priority.zig\").Priority;\nconst IssueType = @import(\"../models/issue_type.zig\").IssueType;\nconst Dependency = @import(\"../models/dependency.zig\").Dependency;\nconst DependencyType = @import(\"../models/dependency.zig\").DependencyType;\nconst Comment = @import(\"../models/comment.zig\").Comment;\n\npub const IssueStoreError = error{\n    IssueNotFound,\n    DuplicateId,\n    InvalidIssue,\n    VersionMismatch,\n};\n\n/// Result of loading the store with corruption tracking.\npub const StoreLoadResult = struct {\n    /// Number of corrupt JSONL entries skipped.\n    jsonl_corruption_count: usize = 0,\n    /// Line numbers of corrupt JSONL entries (1-indexed).\n    jsonl_corrupt_lines: []const usize = &.{},\n\n    pub fn hasCorruption(self: StoreLoadResult) bool {\n        return self.jsonl_corruption_count > 0;\n    }\n\n    pub fn deinit(self: *StoreLoadResult, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n        if (self.jsonl_corrupt_lines.len > 0) {\n            allocator.free(self.jsonl_corrupt_lines);\n        }\n    }\n};\n\npub const IssueStore = struct {\n    allocator: std.mem.Allocator,\n    issues: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(Issue),\n    id_index: std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(usize),\n    dirty_ids: std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(i64),\n    dirty: bool,\n    jsonl_path: []const u8,\n\n    const Self = @This();\n\n    pub fn init(allocator: std.mem.Allocator, jsonl_path: []const u8) Self {\n        return .{\n            .allocator = allocator,\n            .issues = .{},\n            .id_index = .{},\n            .dirty_ids = .{},\n            .dirty = false,\n            .jsonl_path = jsonl_path,\n        };\n    }\n\n    pub fn deinit(self: *Self) void {\n        for (self.issues.items) |*issue| {\n            issue.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n        self.issues.deinit(self.allocator);\n\n        var id_it = self.id_index.keyIterator();\n        while (id_it.next()) |key| {\n            self.allocator.free(key.*);\n        }\n        self.id_index.deinit(self.allocator);\n\n        var dirty_it = self.dirty_ids.keyIterator();\n        while (dirty_it.next()) |key| {\n            self.allocator.free(key.*);\n        }\n        self.dirty_ids.deinit(self.allocator);\n    }\n\n    /// Load issues from the JSONL file into memory.\n    pub fn loadFromFile(self: *Self) !void {\n        var jsonl = JsonlFile.init(self.jsonl_path, self.allocator);\n        const loaded_issues = try jsonl.readAll();\n        defer self.allocator.free(loaded_issues);\n\n        for (loaded_issues) |issue| {\n            const id_copy = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, issue.id);\n            errdefer self.allocator.free(id_copy);\n\n            const idx = self.issues.items.len;\n            try self.issues.append(self.allocator, issue);\n            try self.id_index.put(self.allocator, id_copy, idx);\n        }\n\n        self.dirty = false;\n    }\n\n    /// Load issues from the JSONL file with graceful corruption recovery.\n    /// Logs and skips corrupt entries instead of failing.\n    /// Returns statistics about the load including corruption count.\n    pub fn loadFromFileWithRecovery(self: *Self) !StoreLoadResult {\n        var jsonl = JsonlFile.init(self.jsonl_path, self.allocator);\n        var load_result = try jsonl.readAllWithRecovery();\n        // Take ownership of corrupt_lines before freeing issues slice\n        const corrupt_lines = load_result.corrupt_lines;\n        load_result.corrupt_lines = &.{}; // Prevent double-free\n        errdefer if (corrupt_lines.len > 0) self.allocator.free(corrupt_lines);\n\n        const loaded_issues = load_result.issues;\n        defer self.allocator.free(loaded_issues);\n\n        for (loaded_issues) |issue| {\n            const id_copy = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, issue.id);\n            errdefer self.allocator.free(id_copy);\n\n            const idx = self.issues.items.len;\n            try self.issues.append(self.allocator, issue);\n            try self.id_index.put(self.allocator, id_copy, idx);\n        }\n\n        self.dirty = false;\n\n        return StoreLoadResult{\n            .jsonl_corruption_count = load_result.corruption_count,\n            .jsonl_corrupt_lines = corrupt_lines,\n        };\n    }\n\n    /// Save all issues to the JSONL file.\n    pub fn saveToFile(self: *Self) !void {\n        var jsonl = JsonlFile.init(self.jsonl_path, self.allocator);\n        try jsonl.writeAll(self.issues.items);\n        self.dirty = false;\n\n        // Clear dirty tracking\n        var dirty_it = self.dirty_ids.keyIterator();\n        while (dirty_it.next()) |key| {\n            self.allocator.free(key.*);\n        }\n        self.dirty_ids.clearRetainingCapacity();\n    }\n\n    /// Insert a new issue into the store.\n    pub fn insert(self: *Self, issue: Issue) !void {\n        if (self.id_index.contains(issue.id)) {\n            return IssueStoreError.DuplicateId;\n        }\n\n        const cloned = try issue.clone(self.allocator);\n        errdefer {\n            var c = cloned;\n            c.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        const id_copy = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, cloned.id);\n        errdefer self.allocator.free(id_copy);\n\n        const idx = self.issues.items.len;\n        try self.issues.append(self.allocator, cloned);\n        try self.id_index.put(self.allocator, id_copy, idx);\n\n        try self.markDirty(issue.id);\n    }\n\n    /// Get an issue by ID (without embedded relations).\n    pub fn get(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !?Issue {\n        const idx = self.id_index.get(id) orelse return null;\n        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return null;\n\n        return try self.issues.items[idx].clone(self.allocator);\n    }\n\n    /// Get an issue with all embedded relations (labels, deps, comments).\n    /// Since we store everything in-memory, this just returns the issue as-is.\n    pub fn getWithRelations(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !?Issue {\n        return try self.get(id);\n    }\n\n    /// Get a reference to the stored issue (no clone).\n    /// Caller must NOT free or modify the returned issue.\n    pub fn getRef(self: *Self, id: []const u8) ?*Issue {\n        const idx = self.id_index.get(id) orelse return null;\n        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return null;\n        return &self.issues.items[idx];\n    }\n\n    /// Fields that can be updated on an issue.\n    pub const IssueUpdate = struct {\n        title: ?[]const u8 = null,\n        description: ?[]const u8 = null,\n        design: ?[]const u8 = null,\n        acceptance_criteria: ?[]const u8 = null,\n        notes: ?[]const u8 = null,\n        status: ?Status = null,\n        priority: ?Priority = null,\n        issue_type: ?IssueType = null,\n        assignee: ?[]const u8 = null,\n        owner: ?[]const u8 = null,\n        estimated_minutes: ?i32 = null,\n        closed_at: ?i64 = null,\n        close_reason: ?[]const u8 = null,\n        due_at: ?i64 = null,\n        defer_until: ?i64 = null,\n        external_ref: ?[]const u8 = null,\n        source_system: ?[]const u8 = null,\n        pinned: ?bool = null,\n        is_template: ?bool = null,\n        content_hash: ?[]const u8 = null,\n\n        /// Expected version for optimistic locking.\n        /// If set, update will fail with VersionMismatch if issue.version != expected_version.\n        expected_version: ?u64 = null,\n    };\n\n    /// Update an issue with the given fields.\n    /// If updates.expected_version is set, performs optimistic locking check.\n    pub fn update(self: *Self, id: []const u8, updates: IssueUpdate, now: i64) !void {\n        const idx = self.id_index.get(id) orelse return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n\n        var issue = &self.issues.items[idx];\n\n        // Optimistic locking check\n        if (updates.expected_version) |expected| {\n            if (issue.version != expected) {\n                return IssueStoreError.VersionMismatch;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Increment version on every update\n        issue.version += 1;\n\n        // Update timestamp\n        issue.updated_at = Rfc3339Timestamp{ .value = now };\n\n        // Apply updates\n        if (updates.title) |v| {\n            self.allocator.free(issue.title);\n            issue.title = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n        }\n        if (updates.description) |v| {\n            if (issue.description) |d| self.allocator.free(d);\n            issue.description = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n        }\n        if (updates.design) |v| {\n            if (issue.design) |d| self.allocator.free(d);\n            issue.design = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n        }\n        if (updates.acceptance_criteria) |v| {\n            if (issue.acceptance_criteria) |a| self.allocator.free(a);\n            issue.acceptance_criteria = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n        }\n        if (updates.notes) |v| {\n            if (issue.notes) |n| self.allocator.free(n);\n            issue.notes = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n        }\n        if (updates.status) |v| {\n            freeStatus(issue.status, self.allocator);\n            issue.status = try cloneStatus(v, self.allocator);\n        }\n        if (updates.priority) |v| {\n            issue.priority = v;\n        }\n        if (updates.issue_type) |v| {\n            freeIssueType(issue.issue_type, self.allocator);\n            issue.issue_type = try cloneIssueType(v, self.allocator);\n        }\n        if (updates.assignee) |v| {\n            if (issue.assignee) |a| self.allocator.free(a);\n            issue.assignee = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n        }\n        if (updates.owner) |v| {\n            if (issue.owner) |o| self.allocator.free(o);\n            issue.owner = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n        }\n        if (updates.estimated_minutes) |v| {\n            issue.estimated_minutes = v;\n        }\n        if (updates.closed_at) |v| {\n            issue.closed_at = OptionalRfc3339Timestamp{ .value = v };\n        }\n        if (updates.close_reason) |v| {\n            if (issue.close_reason) |r| self.allocator.free(r);\n            issue.close_reason = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n        }\n        if (updates.due_at) |v| {\n            issue.due_at = OptionalRfc3339Timestamp{ .value = v };\n        }\n        if (updates.defer_until) |v| {\n            issue.defer_until = OptionalRfc3339Timestamp{ .value = v };\n        }\n        if (updates.external_ref) |v| {\n            if (issue.external_ref) |e| self.allocator.free(e);\n            issue.external_ref = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n        }\n        if (updates.source_system) |v| {\n            if (issue.source_system) |s| self.allocator.free(s);\n            issue.source_system = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n        }\n        if (updates.pinned) |v| {\n            issue.pinned = v;\n        }\n        if (updates.is_template) |v| {\n            issue.is_template = v;\n        }\n        if (updates.content_hash) |v| {\n            if (issue.content_hash) |h| self.allocator.free(h);\n            issue.content_hash = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, v);\n        }\n\n        try self.markDirty(id);\n    }\n\n    /// Soft delete an issue by setting its status to tombstone.\n    pub fn delete(self: *Self, id: []const u8, now: i64) !void {\n        try self.update(id, .{ .status = .tombstone }, now);\n    }\n\n    /// Filters for listing issues.\n    pub const ListFilters = struct {\n        status: ?Status = null,\n        priority: ?Priority = null,\n        issue_type: ?IssueType = null,\n        assignee: ?[]const u8 = null,\n        label: ?[]const u8 = null,\n        include_tombstones: bool = false,\n        limit: ?u32 = null,\n        offset: ?u32 = null,\n        order_by: OrderBy = .created_at,\n        order_desc: bool = true,\n\n        pub const OrderBy = enum {\n            created_at,\n            updated_at,\n            priority,\n        };\n    };\n\n    /// List issues with optional filters.\n    pub fn list(self: *Self, filters: ListFilters) ![]Issue {\n        var results: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(Issue) = .{};\n        errdefer {\n            for (results.items) |*issue| {\n                issue.deinit(self.allocator);\n            }\n            results.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        for (self.issues.items) |issue| {\n            // Filter tombstones\n            if (!filters.include_tombstones and statusEql(issue.status, .tombstone)) {\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            // Apply filters\n            if (filters.status) |s| {\n                if (!statusEql(issue.status, s)) continue;\n            }\n            if (filters.priority) |p| {\n                if (issue.priority.value != p.value) continue;\n            }\n            if (filters.issue_type) |t| {\n                if (!issueTypeEql(issue.issue_type, t)) continue;\n            }\n            if (filters.assignee) |a| {\n                if (issue.assignee == null) continue;\n                if (!std.mem.eql(u8, issue.assignee.?, a)) continue;\n            }\n            if (filters.label) |lbl| {\n                var found = false;\n                for (issue.labels) |label| {\n                    if (std.mem.eql(u8, label, lbl)) {\n                        found = true;\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n                if (!found) continue;\n            }\n\n            try results.append(self.allocator, try issue.clone(self.allocator));\n        }\n\n        // Sort\n        const SortContext = struct {\n            order_by: ListFilters.OrderBy,\n            order_desc: bool,\n        };\n        const ctx = SortContext{ .order_by = filters.order_by, .order_desc = filters.order_desc };\n\n        std.mem.sortUnstable(Issue, results.items, ctx, struct {\n            fn lessThan(c: SortContext, a: Issue, b: Issue) bool {\n                const cmp: i64 = switch (c.order_by) {\n                    .created_at => a.created_at.value - b.created_at.value,\n                    .updated_at => a.updated_at.value - b.updated_at.value,\n                    .priority => @as(i64, a.priority.value) - @as(i64, b.priority.value),\n                };\n                return if (c.order_desc) cmp > 0 else cmp < 0;\n            }\n        }.lessThan);\n\n        // Apply offset and limit\n        var start: usize = 0;\n        if (filters.offset) |off| {\n            start = @min(off, results.items.len);\n        }\n\n        var end: usize = results.items.len;\n        if (filters.limit) |lim| {\n            end = @min(start + lim, results.items.len);\n        }\n\n        // Free items outside the range\n        for (results.items[0..start]) |*issue| {\n            issue.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n        for (results.items[end..]) |*issue| {\n            issue.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        // Return slice\n        const slice = try self.allocator.dupe(Issue, results.items[start..end]);\n        results.deinit(self.allocator);\n        return slice;\n    }\n\n    /// Result from counting issues.\n    pub const CountResult = struct {\n        key: []const u8,\n        count: u64,\n    };\n\n    /// Count issues, optionally grouped by a field.\n    pub fn count(self: *Self, group_by: ?GroupBy) ![]CountResult {\n        var counts: std.StringHashMapUnmanaged(u64) = .{};\n        defer counts.deinit(self.allocator);\n\n        for (self.issues.items) |issue| {\n            if (statusEql(issue.status, .tombstone)) continue;\n\n            const key_str: []const u8 = if (group_by) |g| switch (g) {\n                .status => issue.status.toString(),\n                .priority => switch (issue.priority.value) {\n                    0 => \"0\",\n                    1 => \"1\",\n                    2 => \"2\",\n                    3 => \"3\",\n                    4 => \"4\",\n                    else => unreachable,\n                },\n                .issue_type => issue.issue_type.toString(),\n                .assignee => issue.assignee orelse \"(unassigned)\",\n            } else \"total\";\n\n            const entry = counts.getOrPutValue(self.allocator, key_str, 0) catch continue;\n            entry.value_ptr.* += 1;\n        }\n\n        var results: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(CountResult) = .{};\n        errdefer {\n            for (results.items) |r| {\n                self.allocator.free(r.key);\n            }\n            results.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        var it = counts.iterator();\n        while (it.next()) |entry| {\n            const key = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, entry.key_ptr.*);\n            try results.append(self.allocator, .{ .key = key, .count = entry.value_ptr.* });\n        }\n\n        return results.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator);\n    }\n\n    pub const GroupBy = enum {\n        status,\n        priority,\n        issue_type,\n        assignee,\n    };\n\n    /// Check if an issue exists.\n    pub fn exists(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !bool {\n        return self.id_index.contains(id);\n    }\n\n    /// Get labels for an issue.\n    pub fn getLabels(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8) ![]const []const u8 {\n        const idx = self.id_index.get(issue_id) orelse return &[_][]const u8{};\n        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return &[_][]const u8{};\n\n        const issue = self.issues.items[idx];\n        if (issue.labels.len == 0) return &[_][]const u8{};\n\n        const labels = try self.allocator.alloc([]const u8, issue.labels.len);\n        errdefer self.allocator.free(labels);\n\n        for (issue.labels, 0..) |label, i| {\n            labels[i] = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, label);\n        }\n        return labels;\n    }\n\n    /// Add a label to an issue.\n    pub fn addLabel(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8, label: []const u8) !void {\n        const idx = self.id_index.get(issue_id) orelse return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n\n        var issue = &self.issues.items[idx];\n\n        // Check if already exists\n        for (issue.labels) |existing| {\n            if (std.mem.eql(u8, existing, label)) return;\n        }\n\n        // Add new label\n        const label_copy = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, label);\n        errdefer self.allocator.free(label_copy);\n\n        const new_labels = try self.allocator.alloc([]const u8, issue.labels.len + 1);\n        @memcpy(new_labels[0..issue.labels.len], issue.labels);\n        new_labels[issue.labels.len] = label_copy;\n\n        if (issue.labels.len > 0) {\n            self.allocator.free(issue.labels);\n        }\n        issue.labels = new_labels;\n\n        try self.markDirty(issue_id);\n    }\n\n    /// Remove a label from an issue.\n    pub fn removeLabel(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8, label: []const u8) !void {\n        const idx = self.id_index.get(issue_id) orelse return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n\n        var issue = &self.issues.items[idx];\n\n        var found_idx: ?usize = null;\n        for (issue.labels, 0..) |existing, i| {\n            if (std.mem.eql(u8, existing, label)) {\n                found_idx = i;\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (found_idx) |fi| {\n            self.allocator.free(issue.labels[fi]);\n\n            if (issue.labels.len == 1) {\n                self.allocator.free(issue.labels);\n                issue.labels = &[_][]const u8{};\n            } else {\n                const new_labels = try self.allocator.alloc([]const u8, issue.labels.len - 1);\n                var j: usize = 0;\n                for (issue.labels, 0..) |lbl, i| {\n                    if (i != fi) {\n                        new_labels[j] = lbl;\n                        j += 1;\n                    }\n                }\n                self.allocator.free(issue.labels);\n                issue.labels = new_labels;\n            }\n\n            try self.markDirty(issue_id);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get dependencies for an issue.\n    pub fn getDependencies(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8) ![]const Dependency {\n        const idx = self.id_index.get(issue_id) orelse return &[_]Dependency{};\n        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return &[_]Dependency{};\n\n        const issue = self.issues.items[idx];\n        if (issue.dependencies.len == 0) return &[_]Dependency{};\n\n        const deps = try self.allocator.alloc(Dependency, issue.dependencies.len);\n        errdefer self.allocator.free(deps);\n\n        for (issue.dependencies, 0..) |dep, i| {\n            deps[i] = try cloneDependency(dep, self.allocator);\n        }\n        return deps;\n    }\n\n    /// Get comments for an issue.\n    pub fn getComments(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8) ![]const Comment {\n        const idx = self.id_index.get(issue_id) orelse return &[_]Comment{};\n        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return &[_]Comment{};\n\n        const issue = self.issues.items[idx];\n        if (issue.comments.len == 0) return &[_]Comment{};\n\n        const comments = try self.allocator.alloc(Comment, issue.comments.len);\n        errdefer self.allocator.free(comments);\n\n        for (issue.comments, 0..) |c, i| {\n            comments[i] = try cloneComment(c, self.allocator);\n        }\n        return comments;\n    }\n\n    /// Add a comment to an issue.\n    pub fn addComment(self: *Self, issue_id: []const u8, comment: Comment) !void {\n        const idx = self.id_index.get(issue_id) orelse return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n        if (idx >= self.issues.items.len) return IssueStoreError.IssueNotFound;\n\n        var issue = &self.issues.items[idx];\n\n        const cloned = try cloneComment(comment, self.allocator);\n        errdefer freeComment(@constCast(&cloned), self.allocator);\n\n        const new_comments = try self.allocator.alloc(Comment, issue.comments.len + 1);\n        @memcpy(new_comments[0..issue.comments.len], issue.comments);\n        new_comments[issue.comments.len] = cloned;\n\n        if (issue.comments.len > 0) {\n            self.allocator.free(issue.comments);\n        }\n        issue.comments = new_comments;\n\n        try self.markDirty(issue_id);\n    }\n\n    /// Mark an issue as dirty for sync.\n    pub fn markDirty(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n        self.dirty = true;\n        const now = std.time.timestamp();\n\n        if (!self.dirty_ids.contains(id)) {\n            const id_copy = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, id);\n            try self.dirty_ids.put(self.allocator, id_copy, now);\n        } else {\n            self.dirty_ids.getPtr(id).?.* = now;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Clear dirty flag for an issue.\n    pub fn clearDirty(self: *Self, id: []const u8) !void {\n        if (self.dirty_ids.fetchRemove(id)) |kv| {\n            self.allocator.free(kv.key);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /// Get all dirty issue IDs.\n    pub fn getDirtyIds(self: *Self) ![][]const u8 {\n        var ids: std.ArrayListUnmanaged([]const u8) = .{};\n        errdefer {\n            for (ids.items) |id| {\n                self.allocator.free(id);\n            }\n            ids.deinit(self.allocator);\n        }\n\n        var it = self.dirty_ids.keyIterator();\n        while (it.next()) |key| {\n            const id = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, key.*);\n            try ids.append(self.allocator, id);\n        }\n\n        return ids.toOwnedSlice(self.allocator);\n    }\n\n    /// Check if the store has unsaved changes.\n    pub fn isDirty(self: *Self) bool {\n        return self.dirty;\n    }\n\n    /// Get total number of issues (excluding tombstones).\n    pub fn countTotal(self: *Self) usize {\n        var total: usize = 0;\n        for (self.issues.items) |issue| {\n            if (!statusEql(issue.status, .tombstone)) {\n                total += 1;\n            }\n        }\n        return total;\n    }\n\n    /// Get all issues as a slice (no clone, read-only).\n    pub fn getAllRef(self: *Self) []const Issue {\n        return self.issues.items;\n    }\n\n    /// Suggestion for similar ID lookup.\n    pub const IdSuggestion = struct {\n        id: []const u8,\n        title: []const u8,\n    };\n\n    /// Find similar IDs when a lookup fails (for \"did you mean\" suggestions).\n    /// Uses prefix matching and Levenshtein-like scoring.\n    /// Returns up to `max_count` suggestions, caller must free.\n    pub fn findSimilarIds(self: *Self, target: []const u8, max_count: usize) ![]IdSuggestion {\n        if (self.issues.items.len == 0) return &[_]IdSuggestion{};\n\n        const Scored = struct {\n            id: []const u8,\n            title: []const u8,\n            score: i32,\n        };\n\n        var candidates: std.ArrayListUnmanaged(Scored) = .{};\n        defer candidates.deinit(self.allocator);\n\n        for (self.issues.items) |issue| {\n            if (statusEql(issue.status, .tombstone)) continue;\n\n            const score = computeSimilarity(target, issue.id);\n            if (score > 0) {\n                try candidates.append(self.allocator, .{\n                    .id = issue.id,\n                    .title = issue.title,\n                    .score = score,\n                });\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (candidates.items.len == 0) return &[_]IdSuggestion{};\n\n        // Sort by score descending\n        std.mem.sortUnstable(Scored, candidates.items, {}, struct {\n            fn lessThan(_: void, a: Scored, b: Scored) bool {\n                return a.score > b.score;\n            }\n        }.lessThan);\n\n        const result_count = @min(max_count, candidates.items.len);\n        var suggestions = try self.allocator.alloc(IdSuggestion, result_count);\n        errdefer self.allocator.free(suggestions);\n\n        for (0..result_count) |i| {\n            suggestions[i] = .{\n                .id = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, candidates.items[i].id),\n                .title = try self.allocator.dupe(u8, candidates.items[i].title),\n            };\n        }\n\n        return suggestions;\n    }\n\n    /// Free suggestions returned by findSimilarIds.\n    pub fn freeSuggestions(self: *Self, suggestions: []IdSuggestion) void {\n        for (suggestions) |s| {\n            self.allocator.free(s.id);\n            self.allocator.free(s.title);\n        }\n        self.allocator.free(suggestions);\n    }\n};\n\n/// Compute similarity score between target and candidate ID.\n/// Higher score = more similar.\nfn computeSimilarity(target: []const u8, candidate: []const u8) i32 {\n    var score: i32 = 0;\n\n    // Exact prefix match (bd-abc matches bd-abc123)\n    if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, candidate, target)) {\n        score += 100;\n    }\n    // Candidate is prefix of target (bd-abc123 starts with bd-abc)\n    else if (std.mem.startsWith(u8, target, candidate)) {\n        score += 80;\n    }\n\n    // Common prefix length\n    var common_prefix: usize = 0;\n    const min_len = @min(target.len, candidate.len);\n    for (0..min_len) |i| {\n        if (target[i] == candidate[i]) {\n            common_prefix += 1;\n        } else {\n            break;\n        }\n    }\n    score += @intCast(common_prefix * 5);\n\n    // Contains target as substring\n    if (std.mem.indexOf(u8, candidate, target) != null) {\n        score += 30;\n    }\n\n    // Similar length bonus\n    const len_diff: i32 = @intCast(@abs(@as(i64, @intCast(target.len)) - @as(i64, @intCast(candidate.len))));\n    if (len_diff <= 2) {\n        score += 10;\n    }\n\n    return score;\n}\n\n// Helper functions\nfn statusEql(a: Status, b: Status) bool {\n    const Tag = std.meta.Tag(Status);\n    const tag_a: Tag = a;\n    const tag_b: Tag = b;\n    if (tag_a != tag_b) return false;\n    return if (tag_a == .custom) std.mem.eql(u8, a.custom, b.custom) else true;\n}\n\nfn issueTypeEql(a: IssueType, b: IssueType) bool {\n    const Tag = std.meta.Tag(IssueType);\n    const tag_a: Tag = a;\n    const tag_b: Tag = b;\n    if (tag_a != tag_b) return false;\n    return if (tag_a == .custom) std.mem.eql(u8, a.custom, b.custom) else true;\n}\n\nfn cloneStatus(status: Status, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !Status {\n    return switch (status) {\n        .custom => |s| Status{ .custom = try allocator.dupe(u8, s) },\n        else => status,\n    };\n}\n\nfn freeStatus(status: Status, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n    switch (status) {\n        .custom => |s| allocator.free(s),\n        else => {},\n    }\n}\n\nfn cloneIssueType(issue_type: IssueType, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !IssueType {\n    return switch (issue_type) {\n        .custom => |s| IssueType{ .custom = try allocator.dupe(u8, s) },\n        else => issue_type,\n    };\n}\n\nfn freeIssueType(issue_type: IssueType, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n    switch (issue_type) {\n        .custom => |s| allocator.free(s),\n        else => {},\n    }\n}\n\nfn cloneDependency(dep: Dependency, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !Dependency {\n    var result: Dependency = undefined;\n\n    result.issue_id = try allocator.dupe(u8, dep.issue_id);\n    errdefer allocator.free(result.issue_id);\n\n    result.depends_on_id = try allocator.dupe(u8, dep.depends_on_id);\n    errdefer allocator.free(result.depends_on_id);\n\n    result.dep_type = switch (dep.dep_type) {\n        .custom => |s| .{ .custom = try allocator.dupe(u8, s) },\n        else => dep.dep_type,\n    };\n\n    result.created_at = dep.created_at;\n    result.created_by = if (dep.created_by) |c| try allocator.dupe(u8, c) else null;\n    result.metadata = if (dep.metadata) |m| try allocator.dupe(u8, m) else null;\n    result.thread_id = if (dep.thread_id) |t| try allocator.dupe(u8, t) else null;\n\n    return result;\n}\n\nfn cloneComment(comment: Comment, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) !Comment {\n    return Comment{\n        .id = comment.id,\n        .issue_id = try allocator.dupe(u8, comment.issue_id),\n        .author = try allocator.dupe(u8, comment.author),\n        .body = try allocator.dupe(u8, comment.body),\n        .created_at = comment.created_at,\n    };\n}\n\nfn freeComment(comment: *Comment, allocator: std.mem.Allocator) void {\n    allocator.free(comment.issue_id);\n    allocator.free(comment.author);\n    allocator.free(comment.body);\n}\n\n// --- Tests ---\n\ntest \"IssueStore insert and get\" {\n    const allocator = delete list ready blocked search stale count dep label comments history audit sync config info stats doctor orphans lint version schema completions\"\n\n    if [[ $cword -eq 1 ]]; then\n        COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$commands\" -- \"$cur\"))\n        return\n    fi\n\n    case ${words[1]} in\n        show|update|close|reopen|delete|comments|history)\n            # Complete with issue IDs\n            local ids=$(bz list --quiet 2>/dev/null)\n            COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$ids\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            ;;\n        dep)\n            if [[ $cword -eq 2 ]]; then\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"add remove list tree cycles\" -- \"$cur\"))\n            else\n                local ids=$(bz list --quiet 2>/dev/null)\n                COMPREPLY=($(compgen -W \"$ids\"
